lemma executable_generalized_clean_multi_epoch_lifecycle:
  exists-trace
  "∃ verifier contract child_id certificate log canonical_transparency_root
     epoch_0 epoch_pk_0 lineage_root_0 epoch_1 epoch_2 epoch_pk_2
     lineage_root_2 #i0 #it1 #it2 #ia.
    ((((((GeneralizedSecurityCompositionInitialized( verifier, contract,
                                                     child_id, certificate, log, 's1',
                                                     canonical_transparency_root, epoch_0, epoch_pk_0,
                                                     lineage_root_0
          ) @ #i0) ∧
         (GeneralizedCompositionEpochTransition( contract, epoch_0, epoch_1
          ) @ #it1)) ∧
        (GeneralizedCompositionEpochTransition( contract, epoch_1, epoch_2
         ) @ #it2)) ∧
       (GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                                  log, 's1', canonical_transparency_root, epoch_2, epoch_pk_2,
                                  lineage_root_2, 'current', 'active', 'canonical'
        ) @ #ia)) ∧
      (#i0 < #it1)) ∧
     (#it1 < #it2)) ∧
    (#it2 < #ia)"
/*
guarded formula characterizing all satisfying traces:
"∃ verifier contract child_id certificate log canonical_transparency_root
   epoch_0 epoch_pk_0 lineage_root_0 epoch_1 epoch_2 epoch_pk_2
   lineage_root_2 #i0 #it1 #it2 #ia.
  (GeneralizedSecurityCompositionInitialized( verifier, contract, child_id,
                                              certificate, log, 's1', canonical_transparency_root, epoch_0,
                                              epoch_pk_0, lineage_root_0
   ) @ #i0) ∧
  (GeneralizedCompositionEpochTransition( contract, epoch_0, epoch_1
   ) @ #it1) ∧
  (GeneralizedCompositionEpochTransition( contract, epoch_1, epoch_2
   ) @ #it2) ∧
  (GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                             log, 's1', canonical_transparency_root, epoch_2, epoch_pk_2,
                             lineage_root_2, 'current', 'active', 'canonical'
   ) @ #ia)
 ∧
  (#i0 < #it1) ∧ (#it1 < #it2) ∧ (#it2 < #ia)"
*/
simplify
solve( !C6AMultiEpochContract( verifier.1, ~contract ) ▶₀ #it1 )
  case Import_Verified_C5C_And_C6A_Contracts
  solve( !C6AMultiEpochContract( verifier.1, ~contract ) ▶₀ #it2 )
    case Import_Verified_C5C_And_C6A_Contracts
    solve( GeneralizedFinalAccepted( ~verifier, ~contract, ~child_id,
                                     ~certificate, ~log, 's1', ~canonical_transparency_root, ~higher_epoch.1,
                                     epoch_pk_2, lineage_root_2, 'current', 'active', 'canonical'
           ) @ #ia )
      case Accept_Clean_Generalized_Composition
      solve( !C5CSecurityContract( ~verifier, ~contract, ~child_id,
                                   ~certificate, ~log, 's1', ~canonical_transparency_root
             ) ▶₀ #ia )
        case Import_Verified_C5C_And_C6A_Contracts
        solve( !C6AMultiEpochContract( ~verifier, ~contract ) ▶₁ #ia )
          case Import_Verified_C5C_And_C6A_Contracts
          solve( CurrentGeneralizedAcceptancePermit( ~verifier, ~contract,
                                                     ~higher_epoch, epoch_pk_2, lineage_root_2
                 ) ▶₄ #ia )
            case Advance_Generalized_Composition_Epoch
            solve( GeneralizedCompositionEpochState( ~verifier, ~contract, ~epoch_0,
                                                     lower_epoch_pk, lower_lineage_root, 'honest'
                   ) ▶₁ #it1 )
              case Accept_Clean_Generalized_Composition
              solve( AdvanceGeneralizedCompositionEpochPermit( ~verifier, ~contract,

lemma executable_generalized_revocation_exception_lifecycle:
  exists-trace
  "∃ verifier contract child_id certificate log canonical_transparency_root
     epoch_0 epoch_pk_0 lineage_root_0 #i0 #iepoch_compromise #irevoke
     #imissing #iaccept_missing #iapply #irevocation_compromise
     #iaccept_compromised.
    ((((((((((((((GeneralizedSecurityCompositionInitialized( verifier,
                                                             contract, child_id, certificate, log, 's1',
                                                             canonical_transparency_root, epoch_0, epoch_pk_0,
                                                             lineage_root_0
                  ) @ #i0) ∧
                 (GeneralizedCompositionVerifierCompromised( verifier, contract, epoch_0
                  ) @ #iepoch_compromise)) ∧

                ) @ #imissing)) ∧
              (GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                                         log, 's1', canonical_transparency_root, epoch_0, epoch_pk_0,
                                         lineage_root_0, 'stale', 'revoked-missing-update', 'canonical'
               ) @ #iaccept_missing)) ∧
             (GeneralizedCurrentRevocationStateApplied( verifier, certificate
              ) @ #iapply)) ∧
            (GeneralizedRevocationVerifierCompromised( verifier, certificate
             ) @ #irevocation_compromise)) ∧
           (GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                                      log, 's1', canonical_transparency_root, epoch_0, epoch_pk_0,
                                      lineage_root_0, 'stale', 'revoked-compromised-verifier', 'canonical'
            ) @ #iaccept_compromised)) ∧
          (#i0 < #iepoch_compromise)) ∧
         (#iepoch_compromise < #irevoke)) ∧
        (#irevoke < #imissing)) ∧
       (#imissing < #iaccept_missing)) ∧
      (#iaccept_missing < #iapply)) ∧
     (#iapply < #irevocation_compromise)) ∧
    (#irevocation_compromise < #iaccept_compromised)"

lemma executable_generalized_forked_transparency_lifecycle:
  exists-trace

     fork_transparency_root epoch_0 epoch_pk_0 lineage_root_0 #i0 #ic #ia.

        ) @ #ic)) ∧

                                 'honest', 'active', 'forked'
       ) @ #ia)) ∧
     (#i0 < #ic)) ∧
    (#ic < #ia)"
/*
guarded formula characterizing all satisfying traces:

   fork_transparency_root epoch_0 epoch_pk_0 lineage_root_0 #i0 #ic #ia.
  (GeneralizedSecurityCompositionInitialized( verifier, contract, child_id,

              solve( GeneralizedCompositionEpochState( ~verifier, ~contract, ~epoch_0,
                                                       ~epoch_pk_0, ~lineage_root_0, 'honest'

  GeneralizedEpochComponentSatisfied( verifier, contract, epoch, epoch_pk,
                                      lineage_root, 'current'
  ),
  GeneralizedSecurityComponentSatisfied( verifier, contract, child_id,
                                         certificate, log, checkpoint, canonical_transparency_root, 'active',
                                         'canonical'
  ),
  GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate, log,
                            checkpoint, canonical_transparency_root, epoch, epoch_pk, lineage_root,
                            'current', 'active', 'canonical'
  )
  ]->
   [
   GeneralizedCompositionEpochState( verifier, contract, epoch, epoch_pk,
                                     lineage_root, 'honest'
   ),
   GeneralizedCertificateStatus( certificate, 'active' )
   ]

  // loop breakers: [2,3]
  /* has exactly the trivial AC variant */

rule (modulo E) Compromise_Generalized_Transparency_Log:
   [
   !C5CSecurityContract( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate, log,
                         checkpoint, canonical_transparency_root
   ),
   CompromiseGeneralizedTransparencyLogPermit( log, certificate, checkpoint,
                                               canonical_transparency_root
   ),
   Fr( ~fork_transparency_root )
   ]
  --[
  GeneralizedTransparencyLogCompromised( log, checkpoint,
                                         canonical_transparency_root
  ),
  GeneralizedConflictingTransparencyRootCreated( log, certificate,
                                                 checkpoint, canonical_transparency_root,
                                                 ~fork_transparency_root
  )
  ]->
   [
   !GeneralizedForkedTransparencyContract( certificate, log, checkpoint,
                                           canonical_transparency_root, ~fork_transparency_root
   ),
   ForkedGeneralizedAcceptancePermit( verifier, contract, certificate, log,
                                      checkpoint, ~fork_transparency_root
   )
   ]

  /* has exactly the trivial AC variant */

   !C5CSecurityContract( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate, log,

   ),
   !C6AMultiEpochContract( verifier, contract ),
   !GeneralizedForkedTransparencyContract( certificate, log, checkpoint,

  ]->
   [

                                     lineage_root, epoch_state
   ),
   GeneralizedCertificateStatus( certificate, 'active' )

lemma executable_generalized_clean_multi_epoch_lifecycle:
  exists-trace
  "∃ verifier contract child_id certificate log canonical_transparency_root
     epoch_0 epoch_pk_0 lineage_root_0 epoch_1 epoch_2 epoch_pk_2
     lineage_root_2 #i0 #it1 #it2 #ia.
    ((((((GeneralizedSecurityCompositionInitialized( verifier, contract,
                                                     child_id, certificate, log, 's1',
                                                     canonical_transparency_root, epoch_0, epoch_pk_0,
                                                     lineage_root_0
          ) @ #i0) ∧
         (GeneralizedCompositionEpochTransition( contract, epoch_0, epoch_1
          ) @ #it1)) ∧
        (GeneralizedCompositionEpochTransition( contract, epoch_1, epoch_2
         ) @ #it2)) ∧
       (GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                                  log, 's1', canonical_transparency_root, epoch_2, epoch_pk_2,
                                  lineage_root_2, 'current', 'active', 'canonical'
        ) @ #ia)) ∧
      (#i0 < #it1)) ∧
     (#it1 < #it2)) ∧
    (#it2 < #ia)"
/*
guarded formula characterizing all satisfying traces:
"∃ verifier contract child_id certificate log canonical_transparency_root
   epoch_0 epoch_pk_0 lineage_root_0 epoch_1 epoch_2 epoch_pk_2
   lineage_root_2 #i0 #it1 #it2 #ia.
  (GeneralizedSecurityCompositionInitialized( verifier, contract, child_id,
                                              certificate, log, 's1', canonical_transparency_root, epoch_0,
                                              epoch_pk_0, lineage_root_0
   ) @ #i0) ∧
  (GeneralizedCompositionEpochTransition( contract, epoch_0, epoch_1
   ) @ #it1) ∧
  (GeneralizedCompositionEpochTransition( contract, epoch_1, epoch_2
   ) @ #it2) ∧
  (GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                             log, 's1', canonical_transparency_root, epoch_2, epoch_pk_2,
                             lineage_root_2, 'current', 'active', 'canonical'
   ) @ #ia)
 ∧
  (#i0 < #it1) ∧ (#it1 < #it2) ∧ (#it2 < #ia)"
*/
by sorry

lemma executable_generalized_stale_epoch_lifecycle:
  exists-trace
  "∃ verifier contract child_id certificate log canonical_transparency_root
     epoch_0 epoch_pk_0 lineage_root_0 epoch_1 #i0 #it #ic #ir #ia.
    ((((((((GeneralizedSecurityCompositionInitialized( verifier, contract,
                                                       child_id, certificate, log, 's1',
                                                       canonical_transparency_root, epoch_0, epoch_pk_0,
                                                       lineage_root_0
            ) @ #i0) ∧
           (GeneralizedCompositionEpochTransition( contract, epoch_0, epoch_1
            ) @ #it)) ∧
          (GeneralizedCompositionVerifierCompromised( verifier, contract, epoch_1
           ) @ #ic)) ∧
         (GeneralizedCompositionEpochRollback( verifier, contract, epoch_1,
                                               epoch_0
          ) @ #ir)) ∧
        (GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                                   log, 's1', canonical_transparency_root, epoch_0, epoch_pk_0,
                                   lineage_root_0, 'stale', 'active', 'canonical'
         ) @ #ia)) ∧
       (#i0 < #it)) ∧
      (#it < #ic)) ∧
     (#ic < #ir)) ∧
    (#ir < #ia)"
/*
guarded formula characterizing all satisfying traces:
"∃ verifier contract child_id certificate log canonical_transparency_root
   epoch_0 epoch_pk_0 lineage_root_0 epoch_1 #i0 #it #ic #ir #ia.
  (GeneralizedSecurityCompositionInitialized( verifier, contract, child_id,
                                              certificate, log, 's1', canonical_transparency_root, epoch_0,
                                              epoch_pk_0, lineage_root_0
   ) @ #i0) ∧
  (GeneralizedCompositionEpochTransition( contract, epoch_0, epoch_1
   ) @ #it) ∧
  (GeneralizedCompositionVerifierCompromised( verifier, contract, epoch_1
   ) @ #ic) ∧
  (GeneralizedCompositionEpochRollback( verifier, contract, epoch_1,
                                        epoch_0
   ) @ #ir) ∧
  (GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                             log, 's1', canonical_transparency_root, epoch_0, epoch_pk_0,
                             lineage_root_0, 'stale', 'active', 'canonical'
   ) @ #ia)
 ∧
  (#i0 < #it) ∧ (#it < #ic) ∧ (#ic < #ir) ∧ (#ir < #ia)"
*/
simplify
solve( !C6AMultiEpochContract( verifier.1, ~contract ) ▶₀ #it )
  case Import_Verified_C5C_And_C6A_Contracts
  solve( !C6AMultiEpochContract( ~verifier, ~contract ) ▶₀ #ic )
    case Import_Verified_C5C_And_C6A_Contracts
    solve( GeneralizedCompositionEpochState( ~verifier, ~contract,
                                             ~higher_epoch, epoch_pk, lineage_root, 'honest'
           ) ▶₁ #ic )
      case Accept_Clean_Generalized_Composition
      solve( CompromiseGeneralizedCompositionVerifierPermit( ~verifier,
                                                             ~contract
             ) ▶₂ #ic )
        case Import_Verified_C5C_And_C6A_Contracts
        solve( !GeneralizedCompositionCompromiseState( ~verifier, ~contract
               ) ▶₁ #ir )
          case Compromise_Generalized_Composition_Verifier
          solve( !GeneralizedCompositionTransition( ~contract, ~epoch_0,
                                                    ~higher_epoch
                 ) ▶₂ #ir )
            case Advance_Generalized_Composition_Epoch
            solve( !GeneralizedEpochRecord( ~contract, ~epoch_0, lower_epoch_pk,
                                            lower_lineage_root
                   ) ▶₃ #ir )
              case Import_Verified_C5C_And_C6A_Contracts
              solve( GeneralizedFinalAccepted( ~verifier, ~contract, ~child_id,
                                               ~certificate, ~log, 's1', ~canonical_transparency_root,
                                               ~epoch_0, ~epoch_pk_0, ~lineage_root_0, 'stale', 'active',
                                               'canonical'
                     ) @ #ia )
                case Accept_Stale_Generalized_Composition
                solve( !C5CSecurityContract( ~verifier, ~contract, ~child_id,
                                             ~certificate, ~log, 's1', ~canonical_transparency_root
                       ) ▶₀ #ia )
                  case Import_Verified_C5C_And_C6A_Contracts
                  solve( !C6AMultiEpochContract( ~verifier, ~contract ) ▶₁ #ia )
                    case Import_Verified_C5C_And_C6A_Contracts
                    solve( !GeneralizedCompositionCompromiseState( ~verifier, ~contract
                           ) ▶₃ #ia )
                      case Compromise_Generalized_Composition_Verifier
                      solve( StaleGeneralizedAcceptancePermit( ~verifier, ~contract ) ▶₅ #ia )
                        case Compromise_Generalized_Composition_Verifier
                        solve( GeneralizedCompositionEpochState( ~verifier, ~contract, ~epoch_0,
                                                                 lower_epoch_pk, lower_lineage_root, 'honest'
                               ) ▶₁ #it )
                          case Accept_Clean_Generalized_Composition
                          solve( AdvanceGeneralizedCompositionEpochPermit( ~verifier, ~contract,
                                                                           ~epoch_0, ~epoch_pk_0,
                                                                           ~lineage_root_0
                                 ) ▶₂ #it )
                            case Import_Verified_C5C_And_C6A_Contracts
                            solve( GeneralizedCompositionEpochState( ~verifier, ~contract,
                                                                     ~higher_epoch, higher_epoch_pk.1,
                                                                     higher_lineage_root.1, 'compromised'
                                   ) ▶₀ #ir )
                              case Accept_Generalized_Composition_Under_Forked_Transparency
                              solve( GeneralizedCompositionEpochState( ~verifier, ~contract,
                                                                       ~higher_epoch, ~higher_epoch_pk,
                                                                       ~higher_lineage_root, 'honest'
                                     ) ▶₂ #vr )
                                case Advance_Generalized_Composition_Epoch
                                solve( GeneralizedCertificateStatus( ~certificate, 'active' ) ▶₃ #vr )
                                  case Accept_Clean_Generalized_Composition_case_1
                                  solve( GeneralizedCompositionEpochState( ~verifier, ~contract, ~epoch_0,
                                                                           ~epoch_pk_0, ~lineage_root_0,
                                                                           'compromised'
                                         ) ▶₂ #ia )
                                    case Roll_Back_Generalized_Composition_One_Epoch
                                    solve( GeneralizedCertificateStatus( ~certificate, 'active' ) ▶₄ #ia )
                                      case Accept_Generalized_Composition_Under_Forked_Transparency
                                      solve( GeneralizedCompositionEpochState( ~verifier, ~contract, ~epoch_0,
                                                                               ~epoch_pk_0, ~lineage_root_0,
                                                                               'honest'
                                             ) ▶₂ #vr.1 )
                                        case Import_Verified_C5C_And_C6A_Contracts
                                        solve( GeneralizedCertificateStatus( ~certificate, 'active'
                                               ) ▶₃ #vr.1 )
                                          case Import_Verified_C5C_And_C6A_Contracts
                                          solve( GeneralizedCompositionEpochState( ~verifier, ~contract,
                                                                                   ~higher_epoch,
                                                                                   higher_epoch_pk.1,
                                                                                   higher_lineage_root.1,
                                                                                   'compromised'
                                                 ) ▶₃ #vr.2 )
                                            case Compromise_Generalized_Composition_Verifier
                                            solve( GeneralizedCertificateStatus( ~certificate, 'active'
                                                   ) ▶₄ #vr.2 )
                                              case Accept_Clean_Generalized_Composition
                                              simplify
                                              solve( GeneralizedCompositionEpochState( ~verifier, ~contract,
                                                                                       ~higher_epoch.1,
                                                                                       higher_epoch_pk.1,
                                                                                       higher_lineage_root.1,
                                                                                       'compromised'
                                                     ) ▶₀ #vr.4 )
                                                case Accept_Generalized_Composition_Under_Forked_Transparency
                                                solve( GeneralizedCompositionEpochState( ~verifier, ~contract,
                                                                                         ~higher_epoch.1,
                                                                                         ~higher_epoch_pk.1,
                                                                                         ~higher_lineage_root.1,
                                                                                         'honest'
                                                       ) ▶₂ #vr.4 )
                                                  case Advance_Generalized_Composition_Epoch
                                                  solve( GeneralizedCertificateStatus( ~certificate, 'active'
                                                         ) ▶₃ #vr.4 )
                                                    case Accept_Clean_Generalized_Composition_case_1
                                                    SOLVED // trace found
                                                  qed
                                                qed
                                              qed
                                            qed
                                          qed
                                        qed
                                      qed
                                    qed
                                  qed
                                qed
                              qed
                            qed
                          qed
                        qed
                      qed
                    qed
                  qed
                qed
              qed
            qed
          qed
        qed
      qed
    qed
  qed
qed

lemma executable_generalized_revocation_exception_lifecycle:
  exists-trace
  "∃ verifier contract child_id certificate log canonical_transparency_root
     epoch_0 epoch_pk_0 lineage_root_0 #i0 #iepoch_compromise #irevoke
     #imissing #iaccept_missing #iapply #irevocation_compromise
     #iaccept_compromised.
    ((((((((((((((GeneralizedSecurityCompositionInitialized( verifier,
                                                             contract, child_id, certificate, log, 's1',
                                                             canonical_transparency_root, epoch_0, epoch_pk_0,
                                                             lineage_root_0
                  ) @ #i0) ∧
                 (GeneralizedCompositionVerifierCompromised( verifier, contract, epoch_0
                  ) @ #iepoch_compromise)) ∧
                (GeneralizedCertificateRevoked( verifier, certificate ) @ #irevoke)) ∧
               (GeneralizedRevocationUpdateMissing( verifier, certificate
                ) @ #imissing)) ∧
              (GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                                         log, 's1', canonical_transparency_root, epoch_0, epoch_pk_0,
                                         lineage_root_0, 'stale', 'revoked-missing-update', 'canonical'
               ) @ #iaccept_missing)) ∧
             (GeneralizedCurrentRevocationStateApplied( verifier, certificate
              ) @ #iapply)) ∧
            (GeneralizedRevocationVerifierCompromised( verifier, certificate
             ) @ #irevocation_compromise)) ∧
           (GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                                      log, 's1', canonical_transparency_root, epoch_0, epoch_pk_0,
                                      lineage_root_0, 'stale', 'revoked-compromised-verifier', 'canonical'
            ) @ #iaccept_compromised)) ∧
          (#i0 < #iepoch_compromise)) ∧
         (#iepoch_compromise < #irevoke)) ∧
        (#irevoke < #imissing)) ∧
       (#imissing < #iaccept_missing)) ∧
      (#iaccept_missing < #iapply)) ∧
     (#iapply < #irevocation_compromise)) ∧
    (#irevocation_compromise < #iaccept_compromised)"
/*

"∃ verifier contract child_id certificate log canonical_transparency_root

   ]
  --[
  GeneralizedEpochComponentSatisfied( verifier, contract, epoch, epoch_pk,
                                      lineage_root, epoch_state
  ),
  GeneralizedSecurityComponentSatisfied( verifier, contract, child_id,
                                         certificate, log, checkpoint, fork_transparency_root, 'active',
                                         'forked'
  ),
  GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate, log,
                            checkpoint, fork_transparency_root, epoch, epoch_pk, lineage_root,
                            epoch_state, 'active', 'forked'
  )
  ]->
   [
   GeneralizedCompositionEpochState( verifier, contract, epoch, epoch_pk,
                                     lineage_root, epoch_state
   ),
   GeneralizedCertificateStatus( certificate, 'active' )
   ]

  // loop breakers: [3,4]
  /* has exactly the trivial AC variant */

rule (modulo E) Compromise_Generalized_Composition_Verifier:
   [
   !C6AMultiEpochContract( verifier, contract ),
   GeneralizedCompositionEpochState( verifier, contract, epoch, epoch_pk,
                                     lineage_root, 'honest'
   ),
   CompromiseGeneralizedCompositionVerifierPermit( verifier, contract )
   ]
  --[
  GeneralizedCompositionVerifierCompromised( verifier, contract, epoch )
  ]->
   [
   !GeneralizedCompositionCompromiseState( verifier, contract ),
   GeneralizedCompositionEpochState( verifier, contract, epoch, epoch_pk,
                                     lineage_root, 'compromised'
   ),
   StaleGeneralizedAcceptancePermit( verifier, contract )
   ]

  /* has exactly the trivial AC variant */

rule (modulo E) Roll_Back_Generalized_Composition_One_Epoch:
   [
   GeneralizedCompositionEpochState( verifier, contract, higher_epoch,
                                     higher_epoch_pk, higher_lineage_root, 'compromised'
   ),
   !GeneralizedCompositionCompromiseState( verifier, contract ),
   !GeneralizedCompositionTransition( contract, lower_epoch, higher_epoch ),
   !GeneralizedEpochRecord( contract, lower_epoch, lower_epoch_pk,
                            lower_lineage_root
   )
   ]
  --[
  GeneralizedCompositionEpochRollback( verifier, contract, higher_epoch,
                                       lower_epoch
  )
  ]->
   [
   GeneralizedCompositionEpochState( verifier, contract, lower_epoch,
                                     lower_epoch_pk, lower_lineage_root, 'compromised'
   )
   ]

  // loop breaker: [0]
  /* has exactly the trivial AC variant */

rule (modulo E) Accept_Stale_Generalized_Composition:
   [
   !C5CSecurityContract( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate, log,
                         checkpoint, canonical_transparency_root
   ),
   !C6AMultiEpochContract( verifier, contract ),
   GeneralizedCompositionEpochState( verifier, contract, epoch, epoch_pk,
                                     lineage_root, 'compromised'
   ),
   !GeneralizedCompositionCompromiseState( verifier, contract ),
   GeneralizedCertificateStatus( certificate, 'active' ),
   StaleGeneralizedAcceptancePermit( verifier, contract )
   ]
  --[
  GeneralizedEpochCompromiseUsed( verifier, contract, epoch ),
  GeneralizedEpochComponentSatisfied( verifier, contract, epoch, epoch_pk,

  ),

                                         certificate, log, checkpoint, canonical_transparency_root, 'active',
                                         'canonical'
  ),
  GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate, log,
                            checkpoint, canonical_transparency_root, epoch, epoch_pk, lineage_root,
                            'stale', 'active', 'canonical'
  )
  ]->
   [
   GeneralizedCompositionEpochState( verifier, contract, epoch, epoch_pk,
                                     lineage_root, 'compromised'
   ),
   GeneralizedCertificateStatus( certificate, 'active' )
   ]

  // loop breakers: [4,2]
  /* has exactly the trivial AC variant */

rule (modulo E) Revoke_Generalized_Certificate:

   GeneralizedCertificateStatus( certificate, 'active' ),
   RevokeGeneralizedCertificatePermit( verifier, certificate )
   ]

  GeneralizedRevocationUpdatePublished( verifier, certificate )
  ]->
   [
   GeneralizedCertificateStatus( certificate, 'revoked' ),
   ObserveGeneralizedMissingUpdatePermit( verifier, certificate ),
   ApplyGeneralizedRevocationUpdatePermit( verifier, certificate )
   ]

                            checkpoint, canonical_transparency_root, epoch, epoch_pk, lineage_root,
                            'stale', 'revoked-missing-update', 'canonical'
  )
  ]->
   [
   GeneralizedCompositionEpochState( verifier, contract, epoch, epoch_pk,
                                     lineage_root, 'compromised'
   ),
   GeneralizedCertificateStatus( certificate, 'revoked' )
   ]

  // loop breakers: [3,5]
  /* has exactly the trivial AC variant */

rule (modulo E) Accept_Revoked_Generalized_Composition_After_Verifier_Compromise:

                            checkpoint, canonical_transparency_root, epoch, epoch_pk, lineage_root,

  )
  ]->
   [

lemma executable_generalized_clean_multi_epoch_lifecycle:
  exists-trace
  "∃ verifier contract child_id certificate log canonical_transparency_root
     epoch_0 epoch_pk_0 lineage_root_0 epoch_1 epoch_2 epoch_pk_2
     lineage_root_2 #i0 #it1 #it2 #ia.
    ((((((GeneralizedSecurityCompositionInitialized( verifier, contract,
                                                     child_id, certificate, log, 's1',
                                                     canonical_transparency_root, epoch_0, epoch_pk_0,
                                                     lineage_root_0
          ) @ #i0) ∧
         (GeneralizedCompositionEpochTransition( contract, epoch_0, epoch_1
          ) @ #it1)) ∧
        (GeneralizedCompositionEpochTransition( contract, epoch_1, epoch_2
         ) @ #it2)) ∧
       (GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                                  log, 's1', canonical_transparency_root, epoch_2, epoch_pk_2,
                                  lineage_root_2, 'current', 'active', 'canonical'
        ) @ #ia)) ∧
      (#i0 < #it1)) ∧
     (#it1 < #it2)) ∧
    (#it2 < #ia)"
/*
guarded formula characterizing all satisfying traces:
"∃ verifier contract child_id certificate log canonical_transparency_root
   epoch_0 epoch_pk_0 lineage_root_0 epoch_1 epoch_2 epoch_pk_2
   lineage_root_2 #i0 #it1 #it2 #ia.
  (GeneralizedSecurityCompositionInitialized( verifier, contract, child_id,
                                              certificate, log, 's1', canonical_transparency_root, epoch_0,
                                              epoch_pk_0, lineage_root_0
   ) @ #i0) ∧
  (GeneralizedCompositionEpochTransition( contract, epoch_0, epoch_1
   ) @ #it1) ∧
  (GeneralizedCompositionEpochTransition( contract, epoch_1, epoch_2
   ) @ #it2) ∧
  (GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                             log, 's1', canonical_transparency_root, epoch_2, epoch_pk_2,
                             lineage_root_2, 'current', 'active', 'canonical'
   ) @ #ia)
 ∧
  (#i0 < #it1) ∧ (#it1 < #it2) ∧ (#it2 < #ia)"
*/
by sorry

lemma executable_generalized_stale_epoch_lifecycle:

            ) @ #i0) ∧

            ) @ #it)) ∧
          (GeneralizedCompositionVerifierCompromised( verifier, contract, epoch_1
           ) @ #ic)) ∧
         (GeneralizedCompositionEpochRollback( verifier, contract, epoch_1,
                                               epoch_0
          ) @ #ir)) ∧

                                   log, 's1', canonical_transparency_root, epoch_0, epoch_pk_0,
                                   lineage_root_0, 'stale', 'active', 'canonical'
         ) @ #ia)) ∧
       (#i0 < #it)) ∧
      (#it < #ic)) ∧
     (#ic < #ir)) ∧

/*

   epoch_0 epoch_pk_0 lineage_root_0 epoch_1 #i0 #it #ic #ir #ia.
  (GeneralizedSecurityCompositionInitialized( verifier, contract, child_id,
                                              certificate, log, 's1', canonical_transparency_root, epoch_0,

   ) @ #i0) ∧

   ) @ #it) ∧

   ) @ #ic) ∧

                                        epoch_0
   ) @ #ir) ∧
  (GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                             log, 's1', canonical_transparency_root, epoch_0, epoch_pk_0,
                             lineage_root_0, 'stale', 'active', 'canonical'
   ) @ #ia)
 ∧
  (#i0 < #it) ∧ (#it < #ic) ∧ (#ic < #ir) ∧ (#ir < #ia)"
*/
by sorry

lemma executable_generalized_revocation_exception_lifecycle:
  exists-trace
  "∃ verifier contract child_id certificate log canonical_transparency_root
     epoch_0 epoch_pk_0 lineage_root_0 #i0 #iepoch_compromise #irevoke
     #imissing #iaccept_missing #iapply #irevocation_compromise
     #iaccept_compromised.
    ((((((((((((((GeneralizedSecurityCompositionInitialized( verifier,
                                                             contract, child_id, certificate, log, 's1',
                                                             canonical_transparency_root, epoch_0, epoch_pk_0,
                                                             lineage_root_0
                  ) @ #i0) ∧
                 (GeneralizedCompositionVerifierCompromised( verifier, contract, epoch_0
                  ) @ #iepoch_compromise)) ∧
                (GeneralizedCertificateRevoked( verifier, certificate ) @ #irevoke)) ∧
               (GeneralizedRevocationUpdateMissing( verifier, certificate
                ) @ #imissing)) ∧
              (GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                                         log, 's1', canonical_transparency_root, epoch_0, epoch_pk_0,
                                         lineage_root_0, 'stale', 'revoked-missing-update', 'canonical'
               ) @ #iaccept_missing)) ∧
             (GeneralizedCurrentRevocationStateApplied( verifier, certificate
              ) @ #iapply)) ∧
            (GeneralizedRevocationVerifierCompromised( verifier, certificate
             ) @ #irevocation_compromise)) ∧
           (GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                                      log, 's1', canonical_transparency_root, epoch_0, epoch_pk_0,
                                      lineage_root_0, 'stale', 'revoked-compromised-verifier', 'canonical'
            ) @ #iaccept_compromised)) ∧
          (#i0 < #iepoch_compromise)) ∧
         (#iepoch_compromise < #irevoke)) ∧
        (#irevoke < #imissing)) ∧
       (#imissing < #iaccept_missing)) ∧
      (#iaccept_missing < #iapply)) ∧
     (#iapply < #irevocation_compromise)) ∧
    (#irevocation_compromise < #iaccept_compromised)"
/*
guarded formula characterizing all satisfying traces:
"∃ verifier contract child_id certificate log canonical_transparency_root
   epoch_0 epoch_pk_0 lineage_root_0 #i0 #iepoch_compromise #irevoke
   #imissing #iaccept_missing #iapply #irevocation_compromise
   #iaccept_compromised.
  (GeneralizedSecurityCompositionInitialized( verifier, contract, child_id,
                                              certificate, log, 's1', canonical_transparency_root, epoch_0,
                                              epoch_pk_0, lineage_root_0
   ) @ #i0) ∧
  (GeneralizedCompositionVerifierCompromised( verifier, contract, epoch_0
   ) @ #iepoch_compromise) ∧
  (GeneralizedCertificateRevoked( verifier, certificate ) @ #irevoke) ∧
  (GeneralizedRevocationUpdateMissing( verifier, certificate
   ) @ #imissing) ∧
  (GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                             log, 's1', canonical_transparency_root, epoch_0, epoch_pk_0,
                             lineage_root_0, 'stale', 'revoked-missing-update', 'canonical'
   ) @ #iaccept_missing) ∧
  (GeneralizedCurrentRevocationStateApplied( verifier, certificate
   ) @ #iapply) ∧
  (GeneralizedRevocationVerifierCompromised( verifier, certificate
   ) @ #irevocation_compromise) ∧
  (GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                             log, 's1', canonical_transparency_root, epoch_0, epoch_pk_0,
                             lineage_root_0, 'stale', 'revoked-compromised-verifier', 'canonical'
   ) @ #iaccept_compromised)
 ∧
  (#i0 < #iepoch_compromise) ∧
  (#iepoch_compromise < #irevoke) ∧
  (#irevoke < #imissing) ∧
  (#imissing < #iaccept_missing) ∧
  (#iaccept_missing < #iapply) ∧
  (#iapply < #irevocation_compromise) ∧
  (#irevocation_compromise < #iaccept_compromised)"
*/
simplify
solve( !C6AMultiEpochContract( ~verifier, ~contract
       ) ▶₀ #iepoch_compromise )
  case Import_Verified_C5C_And_C6A_Contracts
  solve( GeneralizedCompositionEpochState( ~verifier, ~contract, ~epoch_0,
                                           epoch_pk, lineage_root, 'honest'
         ) ▶₁ #iepoch_compromise )
    case Accept_Clean_Generalized_Composition
    solve( CompromiseGeneralizedCompositionVerifierPermit( ~verifier,
                                                           ~contract
           ) ▶₂ #iepoch_compromise )
      case Import_Verified_C5C_And_C6A_Contracts
      solve( GeneralizedCertificateStatus( ~certificate, 'active'
             ) ▶₀ #irevoke )
        case Accept_Clean_Generalized_Composition_case_1
        solve( RevokeGeneralizedCertificatePermit( ~verifier, ~certificate
               ) ▶₁ #irevoke )
          case Import_Verified_C5C_And_C6A_Contracts
          solve( ObserveGeneralizedMissingUpdatePermit( ~verifier, ~certificate
                 ) ▶₁ #imissing )
            case Revoke_Generalized_Certificate
            solve( ApplyGeneralizedRevocationUpdatePermit( ~verifier, ~certificate
                   ) ▶₁ #iapply )
              case Revoke_Generalized_Certificate
              solve( CompromiseGeneralizedRevocationVerifierPermit( ~verifier,
                                                                    ~certificate
                     ) ▶₀ #irevocation_compromise )
                case Apply_Generalized_Revocation_Update
                solve( GeneralizedFinalAccepted( ~verifier, ~contract, ~child_id,
                                                 ~certificate, ~log, 's1', ~canonical_transparency_root,
                                                 ~epoch_0, ~epoch_pk_0, ~lineage_root_0, 'stale',
                                                 'revoked-missing-update', 'canonical'
                       ) @ #iaccept_missing )
                  case Accept_Revoked_Generalized_Composition_While_Update_Missing
                  solve( !C5CSecurityContract( ~verifier, ~contract, ~child_id,
                                               ~certificate, ~log, 's1', ~canonical_transparency_root
                         ) ▶₀ #iaccept_missing )
                    case Import_Verified_C5C_And_C6A_Contracts
                    solve( !C6AMultiEpochContract( ~verifier, ~contract
                           ) ▶₁ #iaccept_missing )
                      case Import_Verified_C5C_And_C6A_Contracts
                      solve( !GeneralizedMissingUpdateContract( ~verifier, ~certificate
                             ) ▶₂ #iaccept_missing )
                        case Observe_Generalized_Missing_Revocation_Update
                        solve( !GeneralizedCompositionCompromiseState( ~verifier, ~contract
                               ) ▶₄ #iaccept_missing )
                          case Compromise_Generalized_Composition_Verifier
                          solve( MissingUpdateGeneralizedAcceptancePermit( ~verifier, ~certificate
                                 ) ▶₆ #iaccept_missing )
                            case Observe_Generalized_Missing_Revocation_Update
                            solve( GeneralizedFinalAccepted( ~verifier, ~contract, ~child_id,
                                                             ~certificate, ~log, 's1',
                                                             ~canonical_transparency_root, ~epoch_0,
                                                             ~epoch_pk_0, ~lineage_root_0, 'stale',
                                                             'revoked-compromised-verifier', 'canonical'
                                   ) @ #iaccept_compromised )
                              case Accept_Revoked_Generalized_Composition_After_Verifier_Compromise
                              solve( !C5CSecurityContract( ~verifier, ~contract, ~child_id,
                                                           ~certificate, ~log, 's1',
                                                           ~canonical_transparency_root
                                     ) ▶₀ #iaccept_compromised )
                                case Import_Verified_C5C_And_C6A_Contracts
                                solve( !C6AMultiEpochContract( ~verifier, ~contract
                                       ) ▶₁ #iaccept_compromised )
                                  case Import_Verified_C5C_And_C6A_Contracts
                                  solve( !GeneralizedCompromisedRevocationContract( ~verifier, ~certificate
                                         ) ▶₂ #iaccept_compromised )
                                    case Compromise_Generalized_Revocation_Verifier
                                    solve( !GeneralizedCompositionCompromiseState( ~verifier, ~contract
                                           ) ▶₄ #iaccept_compromised )
                                      case Compromise_Generalized_Composition_Verifier
                                      solve( CompromisedRevocationGeneralizedAcceptancePermit( ~verifier,
                                                                                               ~certificate
                                             ) ▶₆ #iaccept_compromised )
                                        case Compromise_Generalized_Revocation_Verifier
                                        solve( GeneralizedCertificateStatus( ~certificate, 'revoked'
                                               ) ▶₀ #imissing )
                                          case Revoke_Generalized_Certificate
                                          solve( GeneralizedCertificateStatus( ~certificate, 'revoked'
                                                 ) ▶₀ #iapply )
                                            case Accept_Revoked_Generalized_Composition_While_Update_Missing
                                            solve( GeneralizedCompositionEpochState( ~verifier, ~contract,
                                                                                     ~epoch_0, ~epoch_pk_0,
                                                                                     ~lineage_root_0, 'honest'
                                                   ) ▶₂ #vr )
                                              case Accept_Generalized_Composition_Under_Forked_Transparency
                                              solve( GeneralizedCertificateStatus( ~certificate, 'active'
                                                     ) ▶₃ #vr )
                                                case Accept_Generalized_Composition_Under_Forked_Transparency
                                                solve( GeneralizedCompositionEpochState( ~verifier, ~contract,
                                                                                         ~epoch_0,
                                                                                         ~epoch_pk_0,
                                                                                         ~lineage_root_0,
                                                                                         'compromised'
                                                       ) ▶₃ #iaccept_missing )
                                                  case Compromise_Generalized_Composition_Verifier
                                                  solve( GeneralizedCertificateStatus( ~certificate, 'revoked'
                                                         ) ▶₅ #iaccept_missing )
                                                    case Observe_Generalized_Missing_Revocation_Update
                                                    solve( GeneralizedCompositionEpochState( ~verifier,
                                                                                             ~contract,
                                                                                             ~epoch_0,
                                                                                             ~epoch_pk_0,
                                                                                             ~lineage_root_0,
                                                                                             'compromised'
                                                           ) ▶₃ #iaccept_compromised )
                                                      case Accept_Revoked_Generalized_Composition_While_Update_Missing
                                                      solve( GeneralizedCertificateStatus( ~certificate,
                                                                                           'revoked'
                                                             ) ▶₅ #iaccept_compromised )
                                                        case Apply_Generalized_Revocation_Update
                                                        solve( GeneralizedCompositionEpochState( ~verifier,
                                                                                                 ~contract,
                                                                                                 ~epoch_0,
                                                                                                 ~epoch_pk_0,
                                                                                                 ~lineage_root_0,
                                                                                                 'honest'
                                                               ) ▶₃ #vr.1 )
                                                          case Import_Verified_C5C_And_C6A_Contracts
                                                          solve( GeneralizedCertificateStatus( ~certificate,
                                                                                               'active'
                                                                 ) ▶₄ #vr.1 )
                                                            case Import_Verified_C5C_And_C6A_Contracts
                                                            SOLVED // trace found
                                                          qed
                                                        qed

   StaleGeneralizedAcceptancePermit( verifier, contract )
   ]

  /* has exactly the trivial AC variant */

rule (modulo E) Roll_Back_Generalized_Composition_One_Epoch:
   [
   GeneralizedCompositionEpochState( verifier, contract, higher_epoch,
                                     higher_epoch_pk, higher_lineage_root, 'compromised'
   ),
   !GeneralizedCompositionCompromiseState( verifier, contract ),
   !GeneralizedCompositionTransition( contract, lower_epoch, higher_epoch ),
   !GeneralizedEpochRecord( contract, lower_epoch, lower_epoch_pk,
                            lower_lineage_root
   )
   ]
  --[
  GeneralizedCompositionEpochRollback( verifier, contract, higher_epoch,
                                       lower_epoch
  )
  ]->
   [
   GeneralizedCompositionEpochState( verifier, contract, lower_epoch,
                                     lower_epoch_pk, lower_lineage_root, 'compromised'
   )
   ]

  // loop breaker: [0]
  /* has exactly the trivial AC variant */

rule (modulo E) Accept_Stale_Generalized_Composition:
   [
   !C5CSecurityContract( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate, log,
                         checkpoint, canonical_transparency_root
   ),
   !C6AMultiEpochContract( verifier, contract ),
   GeneralizedCompositionEpochState( verifier, contract, epoch, epoch_pk,
                                     lineage_root, 'compromised'
   ),
   !GeneralizedCompositionCompromiseState( verifier, contract ),
   GeneralizedCertificateStatus( certificate, 'active' ),
   StaleGeneralizedAcceptancePermit( verifier, contract )
   ]
  --[
  GeneralizedEpochCompromiseUsed( verifier, contract, epoch ),
  GeneralizedEpochComponentSatisfied( verifier, contract, epoch, epoch_pk,
                                      lineage_root, 'stale'
  ),
  GeneralizedSecurityComponentSatisfied( verifier, contract, child_id,
                                         certificate, log, checkpoint, canonical_transparency_root, 'active',
                                         'canonical'
  ),
  GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate, log,
                            checkpoint, canonical_transparency_root, epoch, epoch_pk, lineage_root,
                            'stale', 'active', 'canonical'
  )
  ]->
   [
   GeneralizedCompositionEpochState( verifier, contract, epoch, epoch_pk,
                                     lineage_root, 'compromised'
   ),
   GeneralizedCertificateStatus( certificate, 'active' )
   ]

  // loop breakers: [4,2]
  /* has exactly the trivial AC variant */

rule (modulo E) Revoke_Generalized_Certificate:
   [
   GeneralizedCertificateStatus( certificate, 'active' ),
   RevokeGeneralizedCertificatePermit( verifier, certificate )
   ]
  --[
  GeneralizedCertificateRevoked( verifier, certificate ),
  GeneralizedRevocationUpdatePublished( verifier, certificate )
  ]->
   [
   GeneralizedCertificateStatus( certificate, 'revoked' ),
   ObserveGeneralizedMissingUpdatePermit( verifier, certificate ),
   ApplyGeneralizedRevocationUpdatePermit( verifier, certificate )
   ]

  /* has exactly the trivial AC variant */

rule (modulo E) Observe_Generalized_Missing_Revocation_Update:
   [
   GeneralizedCertificateStatus( certificate, 'revoked' ),
   ObserveGeneralizedMissingUpdatePermit( verifier, certificate )
   ]
  --[ GeneralizedRevocationUpdateMissing( verifier, certificate ) ]->
   [
   GeneralizedCertificateStatus( certificate, 'revoked' ),
   !GeneralizedMissingUpdateContract( verifier, certificate ),
   MissingUpdateGeneralizedAcceptancePermit( verifier, certificate )
   ]

  // loop breaker: [0]
  /* has exactly the trivial AC variant */

rule (modulo E) Accept_Revoked_Generalized_Composition_While_Update_Missing:
   [
   !C5CSecurityContract( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate, log,
                         checkpoint, canonical_transparency_root
   ),
   !C6AMultiEpochContract( verifier, contract ),
   !GeneralizedMissingUpdateContract( verifier, certificate ),
   GeneralizedCompositionEpochState( verifier, contract, epoch, epoch_pk,
                                     lineage_root, 'compromised'
   ),
   !GeneralizedCompositionCompromiseState( verifier, contract ),
   GeneralizedCertificateStatus( certificate, 'revoked' ),
   MissingUpdateGeneralizedAcceptancePermit( verifier, certificate )
   ]
  --[
  GeneralizedEpochCompromiseUsed( verifier, contract, epoch ),
  GeneralizedEpochComponentSatisfied( verifier, contract, epoch, epoch_pk,
                                      lineage_root, 'stale'
  ),
  GeneralizedSecurityComponentSatisfied( verifier, contract, child_id,
                                         certificate, log, checkpoint, canonical_transparency_root,
                                         'revoked-missing-update', 'canonical'
  ),
  GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate, log,
                            checkpoint, canonical_transparency_root, epoch, epoch_pk, lineage_root,
                            'stale', 'revoked-missing-update', 'canonical'
  )
  ]->
   [
   GeneralizedCompositionEpochState( verifier, contract, epoch, epoch_pk,
                                     lineage_root, 'compromised'
   ),
   GeneralizedCertificateStatus( certificate, 'revoked' )
   ]

  // loop breakers: [3,5]
  /* has exactly the trivial AC variant */

rule (modulo E) Apply_Generalized_Revocation_Update:
   [
   GeneralizedCertificateStatus( certificate, 'revoked' ),
   ApplyGeneralizedRevocationUpdatePermit( verifier, certificate )
   ]
  --[ GeneralizedCurrentRevocationStateApplied( verifier, certificate ) ]->
   [
   GeneralizedCertificateStatus( certificate, 'revoked' ),
   CompromiseGeneralizedRevocationVerifierPermit( verifier, certificate )
   ]

  // loop breaker: [0]
  /* has exactly the trivial AC variant */

rule (modulo E) Compromise_Generalized_Revocation_Verifier:
   [ CompromiseGeneralizedRevocationVerifierPermit( verifier, certificate )
   ]
  --[ GeneralizedRevocationVerifierCompromised( verifier, certificate ) ]->
   [
   !GeneralizedCompromisedRevocationContract( verifier, certificate ),
   CompromisedRevocationGeneralizedAcceptancePermit( verifier, certificate )
   ]

  /* has exactly the trivial AC variant */

rule (modulo E) Accept_Revoked_Generalized_Composition_After_Verifier_Compromise:
   [
   !C5CSecurityContract( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate, log,
                         checkpoint, canonical_transparency_root
   ),
   !C6AMultiEpochContract( verifier, contract ),
   !GeneralizedCompromisedRevocationContract( verifier, certificate ),
   GeneralizedCompositionEpochState( verifier, contract, epoch, epoch_pk,
                                     lineage_root, 'compromised'
   ),
   !GeneralizedCompositionCompromiseState( verifier, contract ),
   GeneralizedCertificateStatus( certificate, 'revoked' ),
   CompromisedRevocationGeneralizedAcceptancePermit( verifier, certificate )
   ]
  --[
  GeneralizedEpochCompromiseUsed( verifier, contract, epoch ),
  GeneralizedEpochComponentSatisfied( verifier, contract, epoch, epoch_pk,
                                      lineage_root, 'stale'
  ),
  GeneralizedSecurityComponentSatisfied( verifier, contract, child_id,
                                         certificate, log, checkpoint, canonical_transparency_root,
                                         'revoked-compromised-verifier', 'canonical'
  ),
  GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate, log,
                            checkpoint, canonical_transparency_root, epoch, epoch_pk, lineage_root,
                            'stale', 'revoked-compromised-verifier', 'canonical'
  )
  ]->
   [
   GeneralizedCompositionEpochState( verifier, contract, epoch, epoch_pk,
                                     lineage_root, 'compromised'
   ),
   GeneralizedCertificateStatus( certificate, 'revoked' )
   ]

  // loop breakers: [3,5]
  /* has exactly the trivial AC variant */

lemma executable_generalized_clean_multi_epoch_lifecycle:
  exists-trace
  "∃ verifier contract child_id certificate log canonical_transparency_root
     epoch_0 epoch_pk_0 lineage_root_0 epoch_1 epoch_2 epoch_pk_2
     lineage_root_2 #i0 #it1 #it2 #ia.
    ((((((GeneralizedSecurityCompositionInitialized( verifier, contract,
                                                     child_id, certificate, log, 's1',
                                                     canonical_transparency_root, epoch_0, epoch_pk_0,
                                                     lineage_root_0
          ) @ #i0) ∧
         (GeneralizedCompositionEpochTransition( contract, epoch_0, epoch_1
          ) @ #it1)) ∧
        (GeneralizedCompositionEpochTransition( contract, epoch_1, epoch_2
         ) @ #it2)) ∧
       (GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                                  log, 's1', canonical_transparency_root, epoch_2, epoch_pk_2,
                                  lineage_root_2, 'current', 'active', 'canonical'
        ) @ #ia)) ∧
      (#i0 < #it1)) ∧
     (#it1 < #it2)) ∧
    (#it2 < #ia)"
/*
guarded formula characterizing all satisfying traces:
"∃ verifier contract child_id certificate log canonical_transparency_root
   epoch_0 epoch_pk_0 lineage_root_0 epoch_1 epoch_2 epoch_pk_2
   lineage_root_2 #i0 #it1 #it2 #ia.
  (GeneralizedSecurityCompositionInitialized( verifier, contract, child_id,
                                              certificate, log, 's1', canonical_transparency_root, epoch_0,
                                              epoch_pk_0, lineage_root_0
   ) @ #i0) ∧
  (GeneralizedCompositionEpochTransition( contract, epoch_0, epoch_1
   ) @ #it1) ∧
  (GeneralizedCompositionEpochTransition( contract, epoch_1, epoch_2
   ) @ #it2) ∧
  (GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                             log, 's1', canonical_transparency_root, epoch_2, epoch_pk_2,
                             lineage_root_2, 'current', 'active', 'canonical'
   ) @ #ia)
 ∧
  (#i0 < #it1) ∧ (#it1 < #it2) ∧ (#it2 < #ia)"
*/
by sorry

lemma executable_generalized_stale_epoch_lifecycle:

            ) @ #i0) ∧

            ) @ #it)) ∧
          (GeneralizedCompositionVerifierCompromised( verifier, contract, epoch_1
           ) @ #ic)) ∧
         (GeneralizedCompositionEpochRollback( verifier, contract, epoch_1,
                                               epoch_0
          ) @ #ir)) ∧

                                   log, 's1', canonical_transparency_root, epoch_0, epoch_pk_0,
                                   lineage_root_0, 'stale', 'active', 'canonical'
         ) @ #ia)) ∧
       (#i0 < #it)) ∧
      (#it < #ic)) ∧
     (#ic < #ir)) ∧
    (#ir < #ia)"
/*
guarded formula characterizing all satisfying traces:
"∃ verifier contract child_id certificate log canonical_transparency_root
   epoch_0 epoch_pk_0 lineage_root_0 epoch_1 #i0 #it #ic #ir #ia.
  (GeneralizedSecurityCompositionInitialized( verifier, contract, child_id,
                                              certificate, log, 's1', canonical_transparency_root, epoch_0,
                                              epoch_pk_0, lineage_root_0
   ) @ #i0) ∧
  (GeneralizedCompositionEpochTransition( contract, epoch_0, epoch_1
   ) @ #it) ∧
  (GeneralizedCompositionVerifierCompromised( verifier, contract, epoch_1
   ) @ #ic) ∧
  (GeneralizedCompositionEpochRollback( verifier, contract, epoch_1,
                                        epoch_0
   ) @ #ir) ∧
  (GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                             log, 's1', canonical_transparency_root, epoch_0, epoch_pk_0,
                             lineage_root_0, 'stale', 'active', 'canonical'
   ) @ #ia)
 ∧
  (#i0 < #it) ∧ (#it < #ic) ∧ (#ic < #ir) ∧ (#ir < #ia)"
*/
by sorry

lemma executable_generalized_revocation_exception_lifecycle:
  exists-trace
  "∃ verifier contract child_id certificate log canonical_transparency_root
     epoch_0 epoch_pk_0 lineage_root_0 #i0 #iepoch_compromise #irevoke
     #imissing #iaccept_missing #iapply #irevocation_compromise
     #iaccept_compromised.
    ((((((((((((((GeneralizedSecurityCompositionInitialized( verifier,
                                                             contract, child_id, certificate, log, 's1',
                                                             canonical_transparency_root, epoch_0, epoch_pk_0,
                                                             lineage_root_0
                  ) @ #i0) ∧
                 (GeneralizedCompositionVerifierCompromised( verifier, contract, epoch_0
                  ) @ #iepoch_compromise)) ∧
                (GeneralizedCertificateRevoked( verifier, certificate ) @ #irevoke)) ∧
               (GeneralizedRevocationUpdateMissing( verifier, certificate
                ) @ #imissing)) ∧
              (GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                                         log, 's1', canonical_transparency_root, epoch_0, epoch_pk_0,
                                         lineage_root_0, 'stale', 'revoked-missing-update', 'canonical'
               ) @ #iaccept_missing)) ∧
             (GeneralizedCurrentRevocationStateApplied( verifier, certificate
              ) @ #iapply)) ∧
            (GeneralizedRevocationVerifierCompromised( verifier, certificate
             ) @ #irevocation_compromise)) ∧
           (GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                                      log, 's1', canonical_transparency_root, epoch_0, epoch_pk_0,
                                      lineage_root_0, 'stale', 'revoked-compromised-verifier', 'canonical'
            ) @ #iaccept_compromised)) ∧
          (#i0 < #iepoch_compromise)) ∧
         (#iepoch_compromise < #irevoke)) ∧
        (#irevoke < #imissing)) ∧
       (#imissing < #iaccept_missing)) ∧
      (#iaccept_missing < #iapply)) ∧
     (#iapply < #irevocation_compromise)) ∧
    (#irevocation_compromise < #iaccept_compromised)"
/*
guarded formula characterizing all satisfying traces:
"∃ verifier contract child_id certificate log canonical_transparency_root
   epoch_0 epoch_pk_0 lineage_root_0 #i0 #iepoch_compromise #irevoke
   #imissing #iaccept_missing #iapply #irevocation_compromise
   #iaccept_compromised.
  (GeneralizedSecurityCompositionInitialized( verifier, contract, child_id,
                                              certificate, log, 's1', canonical_transparency_root, epoch_0,
                                              epoch_pk_0, lineage_root_0
   ) @ #i0) ∧
  (GeneralizedCompositionVerifierCompromised( verifier, contract, epoch_0
   ) @ #iepoch_compromise) ∧
  (GeneralizedCertificateRevoked( verifier, certificate ) @ #irevoke) ∧
  (GeneralizedRevocationUpdateMissing( verifier, certificate
   ) @ #imissing) ∧
  (GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                             log, 's1', canonical_transparency_root, epoch_0, epoch_pk_0,
                             lineage_root_0, 'stale', 'revoked-missing-update', 'canonical'
   ) @ #iaccept_missing) ∧
  (GeneralizedCurrentRevocationStateApplied( verifier, certificate
   ) @ #iapply) ∧
  (GeneralizedRevocationVerifierCompromised( verifier, certificate
   ) @ #irevocation_compromise) ∧
  (GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                             log, 's1', canonical_transparency_root, epoch_0, epoch_pk_0,
                             lineage_root_0, 'stale', 'revoked-compromised-verifier', 'canonical'
   ) @ #iaccept_compromised)
 ∧
  (#i0 < #iepoch_compromise) ∧
  (#iepoch_compromise < #irevoke) ∧
  (#irevoke < #imissing) ∧
  (#imissing < #iaccept_missing) ∧
  (#iaccept_missing < #iapply) ∧
  (#iapply < #irevocation_compromise) ∧
  (#irevocation_compromise < #iaccept_compromised)"
*/
by sorry

lemma generalized_acceptance_requires_c5c_and_c6a_contracts:
  all-traces
  "∀ verifier contract child_id certificate log checkpoint
     transparency_root epoch epoch_pk lineage_root epoch_mode revocation_mode
     transparency_mode #ia.
    (GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                               log, checkpoint, transparency_root, epoch, epoch_pk, lineage_root,
                               epoch_mode, revocation_mode, transparency_mode
     ) @ #ia) ⇒
    (∃ canonical_root initial_epoch initial_epoch_pk initial_lineage_root
       #ic5c #ic6a.
      (((C5CContractImported( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate, log,
                              checkpoint, canonical_root
         ) @ #ic5c) ∧
        (C6AContractImported( verifier, contract, initial_epoch,
                              initial_epoch_pk, initial_lineage_root
         ) @ #ic6a)) ∧
       (#ic5c < #ia)) ∧
      (#ic6a < #ia))"
/*
guarded formula characterizing all counter-examples:
"∃ verifier contract child_id certificate log checkpoint
   transparency_root epoch epoch_pk lineage_root epoch_mode revocation_mode
   transparency_mode #ia.
  (GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                             log, checkpoint, transparency_root, epoch, epoch_pk, lineage_root,
                             epoch_mode, revocation_mode, transparency_mode
   ) @ #ia)
 ∧
  ∀ canonical_root initial_epoch initial_epoch_pk initial_lineage_root
    #ic5c #ic6a.
   (C5CContractImported( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate, log,
                         checkpoint, canonical_root
    ) @ #ic5c) ∧
   (C6AContractImported( verifier, contract, initial_epoch,
                         initial_epoch_pk, initial_lineage_root
    ) @ #ic6a)
  ⇒
   ((¬(#ic5c < #ia)) ∨ (¬(#ic6a < #ia)))"
*/
simplify
solve( GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id,
                                 certificate, log, checkpoint, transparency_root, epoch, epoch_pk,
                                 lineage_root, epoch_mode, revocation_mode, transparency_mode
       ) @ #ia )
  case Accept_Clean_Generalized_Composition
  solve( !C5CSecurityContract( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                               log, checkpoint, transparency_root
         ) ▶₀ #ia )
    case Import_Verified_C5C_And_C6A_Contracts
    by contradiction /* from formulas */
  qed
next
  case Accept_Generalized_Composition_Under_Forked_Transparency
  solve( !C5CSecurityContract( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                               log, checkpoint, canonical_transparency_root
         ) ▶₀ #ia )
    case Import_Verified_C5C_And_C6A_Contracts
    by contradiction /* from formulas */
  qed
next
  case Accept_Revoked_Generalized_Composition_After_Verifier_Compromise
  solve( !C5CSecurityContract( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                               log, checkpoint, transparency_root
         ) ▶₀ #ia )
    case Import_Verified_C5C_And_C6A_Contracts
    by contradiction /* from formulas */
  qed
next
  case Accept_Revoked_Generalized_Composition_While_Update_Missing
  solve( !C5CSecurityContract( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                               log, checkpoint, transparency_root
         ) ▶₀ #ia )
    case Import_Verified_C5C_And_C6A_Contracts
    by contradiction /* from formulas */
  qed
next
  case Accept_Stale_Generalized_Composition
  solve( !C5CSecurityContract( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                               log, checkpoint, transparency_root
         ) ▶₀ #ia )
    case Import_Verified_C5C_And_C6A_Contracts
    by contradiction /* from formulas */
  qed
qed

lemma clean_generalized_acceptance_has_complete_evidence:
  all-traces
  "∀ verifier contract child_id certificate log checkpoint
     transparency_root epoch epoch_pk lineage_root #ia.
    (GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                               log, checkpoint, transparency_root, epoch, epoch_pk, lineage_root,
                               'current', 'active', 'canonical'
     ) @ #ia) ⇒
    ((GeneralizedEpochComponentSatisfied( verifier, contract, epoch,
                                          epoch_pk, lineage_root, 'current'
      ) @ #ia) ∧
     (GeneralizedSecurityComponentSatisfied( verifier, contract, child_id,
                                             certificate, log, checkpoint, transparency_root, 'active',
                                             'canonical'
      ) @ #ia))"
/*
guarded formula characterizing all counter-examples:
"∃ verifier contract child_id certificate log checkpoint
   transparency_root epoch epoch_pk lineage_root #ia.
  (GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                             log, checkpoint, transparency_root, epoch, epoch_pk, lineage_root,
                             'current', 'active', 'canonical'
   ) @ #ia)
 ∧
  ((¬(GeneralizedEpochComponentSatisfied( verifier, contract, epoch,
                                          epoch_pk, lineage_root, 'current'
      ) @ #ia)) ∨
   (¬(GeneralizedSecurityComponentSatisfied( verifier, contract, child_id,
                                             certificate, log, checkpoint, transparency_root, 'active',
                                             'canonical'
      ) @ #ia)))"
*/
by sorry

lemma generalized_epoch_compromise_use_requires_prior_compromise:
  all-traces
  "∀ verifier contract epoch #iu.
    (GeneralizedEpochCompromiseUsed( verifier, contract, epoch ) @ #iu) ⇒
    (∃ compromise_epoch #ic.
      (GeneralizedCompositionVerifierCompromised( verifier, contract,
                                                  compromise_epoch
       ) @ #ic) ∧
      (#ic < #iu))"

  (GeneralizedEpochCompromiseUsed( verifier, contract, epoch ) @ #iu)
 ∧
  ∀ compromise_epoch #ic.
   (GeneralizedCompositionVerifierCompromised( verifier, contract,
                                               compromise_epoch
    ) @ #ic)
  ⇒
   ¬(#ic < #iu)"
*/
by sorry

lemma revoked_generalized_acceptance_requires_explicit_exception:
  all-traces
  "∀ verifier contract child_id certificate log checkpoint

                            'stale', 'revoked-compromised-verifier', 'canonical'
  )
  ]->
   [
   GeneralizedCompositionEpochState( verifier, contract, epoch, epoch_pk,
                                     lineage_root, 'compromised'
   ),
   GeneralizedCertificateStatus( certificate, 'revoked' )
   ]

  // loop breakers: [3,5]
  /* has exactly the trivial AC variant */

lemma executable_generalized_clean_multi_epoch_lifecycle:
  exists-trace
  "∃ verifier contract child_id certificate log canonical_transparency_root
     epoch_0 epoch_pk_0 lineage_root_0 epoch_1 epoch_2 epoch_pk_2
     lineage_root_2 #i0 #it1 #it2 #ia.
    ((((((GeneralizedSecurityCompositionInitialized( verifier, contract,
                                                     child_id, certificate, log, 's1',
                                                     canonical_transparency_root, epoch_0, epoch_pk_0,
                                                     lineage_root_0
          ) @ #i0) ∧
         (GeneralizedCompositionEpochTransition( contract, epoch_0, epoch_1
          ) @ #it1)) ∧
        (GeneralizedCompositionEpochTransition( contract, epoch_1, epoch_2
         ) @ #it2)) ∧
       (GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                                  log, 's1', canonical_transparency_root, epoch_2, epoch_pk_2,
                                  lineage_root_2, 'current', 'active', 'canonical'
        ) @ #ia)) ∧
      (#i0 < #it1)) ∧
     (#it1 < #it2)) ∧
    (#it2 < #ia)"
/*
guarded formula characterizing all satisfying traces:
"∃ verifier contract child_id certificate log canonical_transparency_root
   epoch_0 epoch_pk_0 lineage_root_0 epoch_1 epoch_2 epoch_pk_2
   lineage_root_2 #i0 #it1 #it2 #ia.
  (GeneralizedSecurityCompositionInitialized( verifier, contract, child_id,
                                              certificate, log, 's1', canonical_transparency_root, epoch_0,
                                              epoch_pk_0, lineage_root_0
   ) @ #i0) ∧
  (GeneralizedCompositionEpochTransition( contract, epoch_0, epoch_1
   ) @ #it1) ∧
  (GeneralizedCompositionEpochTransition( contract, epoch_1, epoch_2
   ) @ #it2) ∧
  (GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                             log, 's1', canonical_transparency_root, epoch_2, epoch_pk_2,
                             lineage_root_2, 'current', 'active', 'canonical'
   ) @ #ia)
 ∧
  (#i0 < #it1) ∧ (#it1 < #it2) ∧ (#it2 < #ia)"
*/
by sorry
