by sorry

lemma executable_generalized_revocation_exception_lifecycle:
  exists-trace
  "∃ verifier contract child_id certificate log canonical_transparency_root
     epoch_0 epoch_pk_0 lineage_root_0 #i0 #iepoch_compromise #irevoke
     #imissing #iaccept_missing #iapply #irevocation_compromise
     #iaccept_compromised.
    ((((((((((((((GeneralizedSecurityCompositionInitialized( verifier,
                                                             contract, child_id, certificate, log, 's1',
                                                             canonical_transparency_root, epoch_0, epoch_pk_0,
                                                             lineage_root_0
                  ) @ #i0) ∧
                 (GeneralizedCompositionVerifierCompromised( verifier, contract, epoch_0
                  ) @ #iepoch_compromise)) ∧
                (GeneralizedCertificateRevoked( verifier, certificate ) @ #irevoke)) ∧
               (GeneralizedRevocationUpdateMissing( verifier, certificate
                ) @ #imissing)) ∧
              (GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                                         log, 's1', canonical_transparency_root, epoch_0, epoch_pk_0,
                                         lineage_root_0, 'stale', 'revoked-missing-update', 'canonical'
               ) @ #iaccept_missing)) ∧
             (GeneralizedCurrentRevocationStateApplied( verifier, certificate
              ) @ #iapply)) ∧
            (GeneralizedRevocationVerifierCompromised( verifier, certificate
             ) @ #irevocation_compromise)) ∧
           (GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                                      log, 's1', canonical_transparency_root, epoch_0, epoch_pk_0,
                                      lineage_root_0, 'stale', 'revoked-compromised-verifier', 'canonical'
            ) @ #iaccept_compromised)) ∧
          (#i0 < #iepoch_compromise)) ∧
         (#iepoch_compromise < #irevoke)) ∧
        (#irevoke < #imissing)) ∧
       (#imissing < #iaccept_missing)) ∧
      (#iaccept_missing < #iapply)) ∧
     (#iapply < #irevocation_compromise)) ∧
    (#irevocation_compromise < #iaccept_compromised)"
/*
guarded formula characterizing all satisfying traces:
"∃ verifier contract child_id certificate log canonical_transparency_root
   epoch_0 epoch_pk_0 lineage_root_0 #i0 #iepoch_compromise #irevoke
   #imissing #iaccept_missing #iapply #irevocation_compromise
   #iaccept_compromised.
  (GeneralizedSecurityCompositionInitialized( verifier, contract, child_id,
                                              certificate, log, 's1', canonical_transparency_root, epoch_0,
                                              epoch_pk_0, lineage_root_0
   ) @ #i0) ∧
  (GeneralizedCompositionVerifierCompromised( verifier, contract, epoch_0
   ) @ #iepoch_compromise) ∧
  (GeneralizedCertificateRevoked( verifier, certificate ) @ #irevoke) ∧
  (GeneralizedRevocationUpdateMissing( verifier, certificate
   ) @ #imissing) ∧
  (GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                             log, 's1', canonical_transparency_root, epoch_0, epoch_pk_0,
                             lineage_root_0, 'stale', 'revoked-missing-update', 'canonical'
   ) @ #iaccept_missing) ∧
  (GeneralizedCurrentRevocationStateApplied( verifier, certificate
   ) @ #iapply) ∧
  (GeneralizedRevocationVerifierCompromised( verifier, certificate
   ) @ #irevocation_compromise) ∧
  (GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                             log, 's1', canonical_transparency_root, epoch_0, epoch_pk_0,
                             lineage_root_0, 'stale', 'revoked-compromised-verifier', 'canonical'
   ) @ #iaccept_compromised)
 ∧
  (#i0 < #iepoch_compromise) ∧
  (#iepoch_compromise < #irevoke) ∧
  (#irevoke < #imissing) ∧
  (#imissing < #iaccept_missing) ∧
  (#iaccept_missing < #iapply) ∧
  (#iapply < #irevocation_compromise) ∧
  (#irevocation_compromise < #iaccept_compromised)"
*/
by sorry

lemma generalized_acceptance_requires_c5c_and_c6a_contracts:
  all-traces
  "∀ verifier contract child_id certificate log checkpoint
     transparency_root epoch epoch_pk lineage_root epoch_mode revocation_mode
     transparency_mode #ia.
    (GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                               log, checkpoint, transparency_root, epoch, epoch_pk, lineage_root,
                               epoch_mode, revocation_mode, transparency_mode
     ) @ #ia) ⇒
    (∃ canonical_root initial_epoch initial_epoch_pk initial_lineage_root
       #ic5c #ic6a.
      (((C5CContractImported( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate, log,
                              checkpoint, canonical_root
         ) @ #ic5c) ∧
        (C6AContractImported( verifier, contract, initial_epoch,
                              initial_epoch_pk, initial_lineage_root
         ) @ #ic6a)) ∧
       (#ic5c < #ia)) ∧
      (#ic6a < #ia))"
/*
guarded formula characterizing all counter-examples:
"∃ verifier contract child_id certificate log checkpoint
   transparency_root epoch epoch_pk lineage_root epoch_mode revocation_mode
   transparency_mode #ia.
  (GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                             log, checkpoint, transparency_root, epoch, epoch_pk, lineage_root,
                             epoch_mode, revocation_mode, transparency_mode
   ) @ #ia)
 ∧
  ∀ canonical_root initial_epoch initial_epoch_pk initial_lineage_root
    #ic5c #ic6a.
   (C5CContractImported( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate, log,
                         checkpoint, canonical_root
    ) @ #ic5c) ∧
   (C6AContractImported( verifier, contract, initial_epoch,
                         initial_epoch_pk, initial_lineage_root
    ) @ #ic6a)
  ⇒
   ((¬(#ic5c < #ia)) ∨ (¬(#ic6a < #ia)))"
*/
by sorry

lemma clean_generalized_acceptance_has_complete_evidence:
  all-traces
  "∀ verifier contract child_id certificate log checkpoint
     transparency_root epoch epoch_pk lineage_root #ia.
    (GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                               log, checkpoint, transparency_root, epoch, epoch_pk, lineage_root,
                               'current', 'active', 'canonical'
     ) @ #ia) ⇒
    ((GeneralizedEpochComponentSatisfied( verifier, contract, epoch,
                                          epoch_pk, lineage_root, 'current'
      ) @ #ia) ∧
     (GeneralizedSecurityComponentSatisfied( verifier, contract, child_id,
                                             certificate, log, checkpoint, transparency_root, 'active',
                                             'canonical'
      ) @ #ia))"
/*
guarded formula characterizing all counter-examples:
"∃ verifier contract child_id certificate log checkpoint
   transparency_root epoch epoch_pk lineage_root #ia.
  (GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                             log, checkpoint, transparency_root, epoch, epoch_pk, lineage_root,
                             'current', 'active', 'canonical'
   ) @ #ia)
 ∧
  ((¬(GeneralizedEpochComponentSatisfied( verifier, contract, epoch,
                                          epoch_pk, lineage_root, 'current'
      ) @ #ia)) ∨
   (¬(GeneralizedSecurityComponentSatisfied( verifier, contract, child_id,
                                             certificate, log, checkpoint, transparency_root, 'active',
                                             'canonical'
      ) @ #ia)))"
*/
simplify
solve( (¬(GeneralizedEpochComponentSatisfied( verifier, contract, epoch,
                                              epoch_pk, lineage_root, 'current'
          ) @ #ia))  ∥
       (¬(GeneralizedSecurityComponentSatisfied( verifier, contract, child_id,
                                                 certificate, log, checkpoint, transparency_root, 'active',
                                                 'canonical'
          ) @ #ia)) )
  case case_1
  solve( GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id,
                                   certificate, log, checkpoint, transparency_root, epoch, epoch_pk,
                                   lineage_root, 'current', 'active', 'canonical'
         ) @ #ia )
    case Accept_Clean_Generalized_Composition
    by contradiction /* from formulas */
  qed
next
  case case_2
  solve( GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id,
                                   certificate, log, checkpoint, transparency_root, epoch, epoch_pk,
                                   lineage_root, 'current', 'active', 'canonical'
         ) @ #ia )
    case Accept_Clean_Generalized_Composition
    by contradiction /* from formulas */
  qed
qed

lemma generalized_epoch_compromise_use_requires_prior_compromise:

                                                  compromise_epoch
       ) @ #ic) ∧
      (#ic < #iu))"

 ∧

by sorry

by sorry

lemma conflicting_generalized_epoch_histories_require_prior_compromise:

     higher_lineage_root lower_transparency_root higher_transparency_root

                                 log, checkpoint, lower_transparency_root, lower_epoch, lower_epoch_pk,
                                 lower_lineage_root, 'stale', lower_revocation_mode,
                                 lower_transparency_mode
       ) @ #il)) ∧
     (#ih < #il)) ⇒
    (∃ compromise_epoch #ic.
      (GeneralizedCompositionVerifierCompromised( verifier, contract,
                                                  compromise_epoch
       ) @ #ic) ∧
      (#ic < #il))"
/*
guarded formula characterizing all counter-examples:
"∃ verifier contract child_id certificate log checkpoint lower_epoch
   higher_epoch lower_epoch_pk lower_lineage_root higher_epoch_pk
   higher_lineage_root lower_transparency_root higher_transparency_root
   lower_revocation_mode higher_revocation_mode lower_transparency_mode
   higher_transparency_mode #it #ih #il.
  (GeneralizedCompositionEpochTransition( contract, lower_epoch,
                                          higher_epoch
   ) @ #it) ∧
  (GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                             log, checkpoint, higher_transparency_root, higher_epoch, higher_epoch_pk,
                             higher_lineage_root, 'current', higher_revocation_mode,

                                                compromise_epoch

   ⇒
    ¬(#ic < #il))"
*/
by sorry

lemma conflicting_generalized_transparency_roots_require_prior_compromise:
  all-traces
  "∀ verifier_1 verifier_2 contract child_id certificate log checkpoint
     transparency_root_1 transparency_root_2 epoch_1 epoch_2 epoch_pk_1
     epoch_pk_2 lineage_root_1 lineage_root_2 epoch_mode_1 epoch_mode_2
     revocation_mode_1 revocation_mode_2 transparency_mode_1
     transparency_mode_2 #i1 #i2.
    ((((GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier_1, contract, child_id,
                                  certificate, log, checkpoint, transparency_root_1, epoch_1, epoch_pk_1,
                                  lineage_root_1, epoch_mode_1, revocation_mode_1, transparency_mode_1
        ) @ #i1) ∧
       (GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier_2, contract, child_id, certificate,
                                  log, checkpoint, transparency_root_2, epoch_2, epoch_pk_2,
                                  lineage_root_2, epoch_mode_2, revocation_mode_2, transparency_mode_2
        ) @ #i2)) ∧
      (#i1 < #i2)) ∧
     (¬(transparency_root_1 = transparency_root_2))) ⇒
    (∃ canonical_root #ic.
      (GeneralizedTransparencyLogCompromised( log, checkpoint, canonical_root
       ) @ #ic) ∧
      (#ic < #i2))"
/*
guarded formula characterizing all counter-examples:
"∃ verifier_1 verifier_2 contract child_id certificate log checkpoint
   transparency_root_1 transparency_root_2 epoch_1 epoch_2 epoch_pk_1
   epoch_pk_2 lineage_root_1 lineage_root_2 epoch_mode_1 epoch_mode_2
   revocation_mode_1 revocation_mode_2 transparency_mode_1
   transparency_mode_2 #i1 #i2.
  (GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier_1, contract, child_id, certificate,
                             log, checkpoint, transparency_root_1, epoch_1, epoch_pk_1,
                             lineage_root_1, epoch_mode_1, revocation_mode_1, transparency_mode_1
   ) @ #i1) ∧
  (GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier_2, contract, child_id, certificate,
                             log, checkpoint, transparency_root_2, epoch_2, epoch_pk_2,
                             lineage_root_2, epoch_mode_2, revocation_mode_2, transparency_mode_2
   ) @ #i2)
 ∧
  (#i1 < #i2) ∧
  (¬(transparency_root_1 = transparency_root_2)) ∧

              (GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                                         log, 's1', canonical_transparency_root, epoch_0, epoch_pk_0,
                                         lineage_root_0, 'stale', 'revoked-missing-update', 'canonical'
               ) @ #iaccept_missing)) ∧
             (GeneralizedCurrentRevocationStateApplied( verifier, certificate
              ) @ #iapply)) ∧
            (GeneralizedRevocationVerifierCompromised( verifier, certificate
             ) @ #irevocation_compromise)) ∧
           (GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                                      log, 's1', canonical_transparency_root, epoch_0, epoch_pk_0,
                                      lineage_root_0, 'stale', 'revoked-compromised-verifier', 'canonical'
            ) @ #iaccept_compromised)) ∧
          (#i0 < #iepoch_compromise)) ∧
         (#iepoch_compromise < #irevoke)) ∧
        (#irevoke < #imissing)) ∧
       (#imissing < #iaccept_missing)) ∧
      (#iaccept_missing < #iapply)) ∧
     (#iapply < #irevocation_compromise)) ∧
    (#irevocation_compromise < #iaccept_compromised)"
/*

"∃ verifier contract child_id certificate log canonical_transparency_root
   epoch_0 epoch_pk_0 lineage_root_0 #i0 #iepoch_compromise #irevoke

   #iaccept_compromised.
  (GeneralizedSecurityCompositionInitialized( verifier, contract, child_id,
                                              certificate, log, 's1', canonical_transparency_root, epoch_0,
                                              epoch_pk_0, lineage_root_0
   ) @ #i0) ∧
  (GeneralizedCompositionVerifierCompromised( verifier, contract, epoch_0
   ) @ #iepoch_compromise) ∧
  (GeneralizedCertificateRevoked( verifier, certificate ) @ #irevoke) ∧
  (GeneralizedRevocationUpdateMissing( verifier, certificate
   ) @ #imissing) ∧
  (GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                             log, 's1', canonical_transparency_root, epoch_0, epoch_pk_0,

  all-traces

  by contradiction /* from formulas */
qed

   [
   GeneralizedCompositionEpochState( verifier, contract, epoch, epoch_pk,
                                     lineage_root, 'honest'
   ),
   GeneralizedCertificateStatus( certificate, 'active' )
   ]

  // loop breakers: [2,3]
  /* has exactly the trivial AC variant */

rule (modulo E) Compromise_Generalized_Transparency_Log:
   [
   !C5CSecurityContract( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate, log,
                         checkpoint, canonical_transparency_root
   ),
   CompromiseGeneralizedTransparencyLogPermit( log, certificate, checkpoint,
                                               canonical_transparency_root
   ),
   Fr( ~fork_transparency_root )
   ]
  --[
  GeneralizedTransparencyLogCompromised( log, checkpoint,
                                         canonical_transparency_root
  ),
  GeneralizedConflictingTransparencyRootCreated( log, certificate,
                                                 checkpoint, canonical_transparency_root,
                                                 ~fork_transparency_root
  )
  ]->
   [
   !GeneralizedForkedTransparencyContract( certificate, log, checkpoint,
                                           canonical_transparency_root, ~fork_transparency_root
   ),
   ForkedGeneralizedAcceptancePermit( verifier, contract, certificate, log,
                                      checkpoint, ~fork_transparency_root
   )
   ]

  /* has exactly the trivial AC variant */

rule (modulo E) Accept_Generalized_Composition_Under_Forked_Transparency:
   [
   !C5CSecurityContract( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate, log,
                         checkpoint, canonical_transparency_root
   ),
   !C6AMultiEpochContract( verifier, contract ),
   !GeneralizedForkedTransparencyContract( certificate, log, checkpoint,
                                           canonical_transparency_root, fork_transparency_root
   ),
   GeneralizedCompositionEpochState( verifier, contract, epoch, epoch_pk,
                                     lineage_root, epoch_state
   ),
   GeneralizedCertificateStatus( certificate, 'active' ),
   ForkedGeneralizedAcceptancePermit( verifier, contract, certificate, log,
                                      checkpoint, fork_transparency_root
   )
   ]
  --[
  GeneralizedEpochComponentSatisfied( verifier, contract, epoch, epoch_pk,
                                      lineage_root, epoch_state
  ),
  GeneralizedSecurityComponentSatisfied( verifier, contract, child_id,
                                         certificate, log, checkpoint, fork_transparency_root, 'active',
                                         'forked'
  ),
  GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate, log,
                            checkpoint, fork_transparency_root, epoch, epoch_pk, lineage_root,
                            epoch_state, 'active', 'forked'
  )
  ]->
   [
   GeneralizedCompositionEpochState( verifier, contract, epoch, epoch_pk,
                                     lineage_root, epoch_state
   ),
   GeneralizedCertificateStatus( certificate, 'active' )
   ]

  // loop breakers: [3,4]
  /* has exactly the trivial AC variant */

rule (modulo E) Compromise_Generalized_Composition_Verifier:
   [
   !C6AMultiEpochContract( verifier, contract ),
   GeneralizedCompositionEpochState( verifier, contract, epoch, epoch_pk,
                                     lineage_root, 'honest'

   ]

   GeneralizedCompositionEpochState( verifier, contract, epoch, epoch_pk,
                                     lineage_root, 'compromised'
   ),
   StaleGeneralizedAcceptancePermit( verifier, contract )
   ]

  /* has exactly the trivial AC variant */

rule (modulo E) Roll_Back_Generalized_Composition_One_Epoch:
   [
   GeneralizedCompositionEpochState( verifier, contract, higher_epoch,
                                     higher_epoch_pk, higher_lineage_root, 'compromised'
   ),
   !GeneralizedCompositionCompromiseState( verifier, contract ),
   !GeneralizedCompositionTransition( contract, lower_epoch, higher_epoch ),
   !GeneralizedEpochRecord( contract, lower_epoch, lower_epoch_pk,
                            lower_lineage_root
   )
   ]
  --[
  GeneralizedCompositionEpochRollback( verifier, contract, higher_epoch,
                                       lower_epoch
  )
  ]->
   [
   GeneralizedCompositionEpochState( verifier, contract, lower_epoch,
                                     lower_epoch_pk, lower_lineage_root, 'compromised'
   )
   ]

  // loop breaker: [0]
  /* has exactly the trivial AC variant */

rule (modulo E) Accept_Stale_Generalized_Composition:

                         checkpoint, canonical_transparency_root
   ),

  )
  ]->
   [
   GeneralizedCompositionEpochState( verifier, contract, epoch, epoch_pk,
                                     lineage_root, 'compromised'
   ),
   GeneralizedCertificateStatus( certificate, 'active' )
   ]

  // loop breakers: [4,2]
  /* has exactly the trivial AC variant */

lemma executable_generalized_clean_multi_epoch_lifecycle:
  exists-trace
  "∃ verifier contract child_id certificate log canonical_transparency_root
     epoch_0 epoch_pk_0 lineage_root_0 epoch_1 epoch_2 epoch_pk_2
     lineage_root_2 #i0 #it1 #it2 #ia.
    ((((((GeneralizedSecurityCompositionInitialized( verifier, contract,
                                                     child_id, certificate, log, 's1',
                                                     canonical_transparency_root, epoch_0, epoch_pk_0,
                                                     lineage_root_0
          ) @ #i0) ∧
         (GeneralizedCompositionEpochTransition( contract, epoch_0, epoch_1
          ) @ #it1)) ∧
        (GeneralizedCompositionEpochTransition( contract, epoch_1, epoch_2
         ) @ #it2)) ∧
       (GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                                  log, 's1', canonical_transparency_root, epoch_2, epoch_pk_2,
                                  lineage_root_2, 'current', 'active', 'canonical'
        ) @ #ia)) ∧
      (#i0 < #it1)) ∧
     (#it1 < #it2)) ∧
    (#it2 < #ia)"
/*
guarded formula characterizing all satisfying traces:
"∃ verifier contract child_id certificate log canonical_transparency_root
   epoch_0 epoch_pk_0 lineage_root_0 epoch_1 epoch_2 epoch_pk_2
   lineage_root_2 #i0 #it1 #it2 #ia.
  (GeneralizedSecurityCompositionInitialized( verifier, contract, child_id,
                                              certificate, log, 's1', canonical_transparency_root, epoch_0,
                                              epoch_pk_0, lineage_root_0
   ) @ #i0) ∧
  (GeneralizedCompositionEpochTransition( contract, epoch_0, epoch_1
   ) @ #it1) ∧
  (GeneralizedCompositionEpochTransition( contract, epoch_1, epoch_2
   ) @ #it2) ∧
  (GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                             log, 's1', canonical_transparency_root, epoch_2, epoch_pk_2,
                             lineage_root_2, 'current', 'active', 'canonical'
   ) @ #ia)
 ∧
  (#i0 < #it1) ∧ (#it1 < #it2) ∧ (#it2 < #ia)"
*/
by sorry

lemma executable_generalized_revocation_exception_lifecycle:
  exists-trace
  "∃ verifier contract child_id certificate log canonical_transparency_root
     epoch_0 epoch_pk_0 lineage_root_0 #i0 #iepoch_compromise #irevoke
     #imissing #iaccept_missing #iapply #irevocation_compromise
     #iaccept_compromised.
    ((((((((((((((GeneralizedSecurityCompositionInitialized( verifier,
                                                             contract, child_id, certificate, log, 's1',
                                                             canonical_transparency_root, epoch_0, epoch_pk_0,
                                                             lineage_root_0
                  ) @ #i0) ∧
                 (GeneralizedCompositionVerifierCompromised( verifier, contract, epoch_0
                  ) @ #iepoch_compromise)) ∧
                (GeneralizedCertificateRevoked( verifier, certificate ) @ #irevoke)) ∧
               (GeneralizedRevocationUpdateMissing( verifier, certificate
                ) @ #imissing)) ∧
              (GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                                         log, 's1', canonical_transparency_root, epoch_0, epoch_pk_0,
                                         lineage_root_0, 'stale', 'revoked-missing-update', 'canonical'
               ) @ #iaccept_missing)) ∧
             (GeneralizedCurrentRevocationStateApplied( verifier, certificate
              ) @ #iapply)) ∧
            (GeneralizedRevocationVerifierCompromised( verifier, certificate
             ) @ #irevocation_compromise)) ∧
           (GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                                      log, 's1', canonical_transparency_root, epoch_0, epoch_pk_0,
                                      lineage_root_0, 'stale', 'revoked-compromised-verifier', 'canonical'
            ) @ #iaccept_compromised)) ∧
          (#i0 < #iepoch_compromise)) ∧
         (#iepoch_compromise < #irevoke)) ∧
        (#irevoke < #imissing)) ∧
       (#imissing < #iaccept_missing)) ∧
      (#iaccept_missing < #iapply)) ∧
     (#iapply < #irevocation_compromise)) ∧
    (#irevocation_compromise < #iaccept_compromised)"

   #iaccept_compromised.

                                              epoch_pk_0, lineage_root_0
   ) @ #i0) ∧

lemma generalized_acceptance_requires_c5c_and_c6a_contracts:
  all-traces
  "∀ verifier contract child_id certificate log checkpoint
     transparency_root epoch epoch_pk lineage_root epoch_mode revocation_mode
     transparency_mode #ia.
    (GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                               log, checkpoint, transparency_root, epoch, epoch_pk, lineage_root,
                               epoch_mode, revocation_mode, transparency_mode
     ) @ #ia) ⇒
    (∃ canonical_root initial_epoch initial_epoch_pk initial_lineage_root
       #ic5c #ic6a.
      (((C5CContractImported( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate, log,
                              checkpoint, canonical_root
         ) @ #ic5c) ∧
        (C6AContractImported( verifier, contract, initial_epoch,
                              initial_epoch_pk, initial_lineage_root
         ) @ #ic6a)) ∧
       (#ic5c < #ia)) ∧
      (#ic6a < #ia))"
/*
guarded formula characterizing all counter-examples:
"∃ verifier contract child_id certificate log checkpoint
   transparency_root epoch epoch_pk lineage_root epoch_mode revocation_mode
   transparency_mode #ia.
  (GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                             log, checkpoint, transparency_root, epoch, epoch_pk, lineage_root,
                             epoch_mode, revocation_mode, transparency_mode
   ) @ #ia)
 ∧
  ∀ canonical_root initial_epoch initial_epoch_pk initial_lineage_root
    #ic5c #ic6a.
   (C5CContractImported( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate, log,
                         checkpoint, canonical_root
    ) @ #ic5c) ∧
   (C6AContractImported( verifier, contract, initial_epoch,
                         initial_epoch_pk, initial_lineage_root
    ) @ #ic6a)
  ⇒
   ((¬(#ic5c < #ia)) ∨ (¬(#ic6a < #ia)))"
*/
by sorry

                                             'canonical'

                             log, checkpoint, transparency_root, epoch, epoch_pk, lineage_root,

by sorry

lemma stale_generalized_acceptance_uses_epoch_compromise_state:
  all-traces
  "∀ verifier contract child_id certificate log checkpoint
     transparency_root epoch epoch_pk lineage_root revocation_mode
     transparency_mode #ia.
    (GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                               log, checkpoint, transparency_root, epoch, epoch_pk, lineage_root,
                               'stale', revocation_mode, transparency_mode
     ) @ #ia) ⇒
    (GeneralizedEpochCompromiseUsed( verifier, contract, epoch ) @ #ia)"
/*
guarded formula characterizing all counter-examples:
"∃ verifier contract child_id certificate log checkpoint
   transparency_root epoch epoch_pk lineage_root revocation_mode
   transparency_mode #ia.
  (GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                             log, checkpoint, transparency_root, epoch, epoch_pk, lineage_root,
                             'stale', revocation_mode, transparency_mode
   ) @ #ia)
 ∧
  ¬(GeneralizedEpochCompromiseUsed( verifier, contract, epoch ) @ #ia)"
*/
simplify
solve( GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id,
                                 certificate, log, checkpoint, transparency_root, epoch, epoch_pk,
                                 lineage_root, 'stale', revocation_mode, transparency_mode
       ) @ #ia )
  case Accept_Generalized_Composition_Under_Forked_Transparency
  solve( !C5CSecurityContract( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                               log, checkpoint, canonical_transparency_root
         ) ▶₀ #ia )
    case Import_Verified_C5C_And_C6A_Contracts
    solve( !C6AMultiEpochContract( ~verifier, ~contract ) ▶₁ #ia )
      case Import_Verified_C5C_And_C6A_Contracts
      solve( !GeneralizedForkedTransparencyContract( ~certificate, ~log, 's1',
                                                     ~canonical_transparency_root, transparency_root
             ) ▶₂ #ia )
        case Compromise_Generalized_Transparency_Log
        solve( ForkedGeneralizedAcceptancePermit( ~verifier, ~contract,
                                                  ~certificate, ~log, 's1', ~fork_transparency_root
               ) ▶₅ #ia )
          case Compromise_Generalized_Transparency_Log
          solve( GeneralizedCompositionEpochState( ~verifier, ~contract, epoch,
                                                   epoch_pk, lineage_root, 'stale'
                 ) ▶₃ #ia )
            case Accept_Generalized_Composition_Under_Forked_Transparency
            by contradiction /* cyclic */
          qed
        qed
      qed
    qed
  qed
next
  case Accept_Revoked_Generalized_Composition_After_Verifier_Compromise
  by contradiction /* from formulas */
next
  case Accept_Revoked_Generalized_Composition_While_Update_Missing
  by contradiction /* from formulas */
next
  case Accept_Stale_Generalized_Composition
  by contradiction /* from formulas */
qed

by sorry

   !C6AMultiEpochContract( verifier, contract ),
   !GeneralizedMissingUpdateContract( verifier, certificate ),
   GeneralizedCompositionEpochState( verifier, contract, epoch, epoch_pk,
                                     lineage_root, 'compromised'
   ),
   !GeneralizedCompositionCompromiseState( verifier, contract ),
   GeneralizedCertificateStatus( certificate, 'revoked' ),
   MissingUpdateGeneralizedAcceptancePermit( verifier, certificate )
   ]
  --[
  GeneralizedEpochCompromiseUsed( verifier, contract, epoch ),
  GeneralizedEpochComponentSatisfied( verifier, contract, epoch, epoch_pk,
                                      lineage_root, 'stale'
  ),
  GeneralizedSecurityComponentSatisfied( verifier, contract, child_id,
                                         certificate, log, checkpoint, canonical_transparency_root,
                                         'revoked-missing-update', 'canonical'
  ),
  GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate, log,
                            checkpoint, canonical_transparency_root, epoch, epoch_pk, lineage_root,
                            'stale', 'revoked-missing-update', 'canonical'
  )
  ]->
   [
   GeneralizedCompositionEpochState( verifier, contract, epoch, epoch_pk,
                                     lineage_root, 'compromised'
   ),
   GeneralizedCertificateStatus( certificate, 'revoked' )
   ]

  // loop breakers: [3,5]
  /* has exactly the trivial AC variant */

rule (modulo E) Apply_Generalized_Revocation_Update:
   [
   GeneralizedCertificateStatus( certificate, 'revoked' ),
   ApplyGeneralizedRevocationUpdatePermit( verifier, certificate )
   ]
  --[ GeneralizedCurrentRevocationStateApplied( verifier, certificate ) ]->
   [
   GeneralizedCertificateStatus( certificate, 'revoked' ),
   CompromiseGeneralizedRevocationVerifierPermit( verifier, certificate )
   ]

  // loop breaker: [0]
  /* has exactly the trivial AC variant */

rule (modulo E) Compromise_Generalized_Revocation_Verifier:
   [ CompromiseGeneralizedRevocationVerifierPermit( verifier, certificate )
   ]
  --[ GeneralizedRevocationVerifierCompromised( verifier, certificate ) ]->
   [
   !GeneralizedCompromisedRevocationContract( verifier, certificate ),
   CompromisedRevocationGeneralizedAcceptancePermit( verifier, certificate )
   ]

  /* has exactly the trivial AC variant */

rule (modulo E) Accept_Revoked_Generalized_Composition_After_Verifier_Compromise:
   [
   !C5CSecurityContract( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate, log,
                         checkpoint, canonical_transparency_root
   ),
   !C6AMultiEpochContract( verifier, contract ),
   !GeneralizedCompromisedRevocationContract( verifier, certificate ),
   GeneralizedCompositionEpochState( verifier, contract, epoch, epoch_pk,
                                     lineage_root, 'compromised'
   ),
   !GeneralizedCompositionCompromiseState( verifier, contract ),
   GeneralizedCertificateStatus( certificate, 'revoked' ),
   CompromisedRevocationGeneralizedAcceptancePermit( verifier, certificate )
   ]
  --[
  GeneralizedEpochCompromiseUsed( verifier, contract, epoch ),
  GeneralizedEpochComponentSatisfied( verifier, contract, epoch, epoch_pk,
                                      lineage_root, 'stale'
  ),
  GeneralizedSecurityComponentSatisfied( verifier, contract, child_id,
                                         certificate, log, checkpoint, canonical_transparency_root,
                                         'revoked-compromised-verifier', 'canonical'
  ),
  GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate, log,
                            checkpoint, canonical_transparency_root, epoch, epoch_pk, lineage_root,
                            'stale', 'revoked-compromised-verifier', 'canonical'
  )
  ]->
   [
   GeneralizedCompositionEpochState( verifier, contract, epoch, epoch_pk,
                                     lineage_root, 'compromised'
   ),
   GeneralizedCertificateStatus( certificate, 'revoked' )
   ]

  // loop breakers: [3,5]
  /* has exactly the trivial AC variant */

lemma executable_generalized_clean_multi_epoch_lifecycle:
  exists-trace
  "∃ verifier contract child_id certificate log canonical_transparency_root
     epoch_0 epoch_pk_0 lineage_root_0 epoch_1 epoch_2 epoch_pk_2
     lineage_root_2 #i0 #it1 #it2 #ia.
    ((((((GeneralizedSecurityCompositionInitialized( verifier, contract,
                                                     child_id, certificate, log, 's1',
                                                     canonical_transparency_root, epoch_0, epoch_pk_0,
                                                     lineage_root_0
          ) @ #i0) ∧
         (GeneralizedCompositionEpochTransition( contract, epoch_0, epoch_1
          ) @ #it1)) ∧
        (GeneralizedCompositionEpochTransition( contract, epoch_1, epoch_2
         ) @ #it2)) ∧
       (GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                                  log, 's1', canonical_transparency_root, epoch_2, epoch_pk_2,
                                  lineage_root_2, 'current', 'active', 'canonical'
        ) @ #ia)) ∧
      (#i0 < #it1)) ∧
     (#it1 < #it2)) ∧
    (#it2 < #ia)"
/*
guarded formula characterizing all satisfying traces:
"∃ verifier contract child_id certificate log canonical_transparency_root
   epoch_0 epoch_pk_0 lineage_root_0 epoch_1 epoch_2 epoch_pk_2
   lineage_root_2 #i0 #it1 #it2 #ia.
  (GeneralizedSecurityCompositionInitialized( verifier, contract, child_id,
                                              certificate, log, 's1', canonical_transparency_root, epoch_0,
                                              epoch_pk_0, lineage_root_0
   ) @ #i0) ∧
  (GeneralizedCompositionEpochTransition( contract, epoch_0, epoch_1
   ) @ #it1) ∧
  (GeneralizedCompositionEpochTransition( contract, epoch_1, epoch_2
   ) @ #it2) ∧
  (GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                             log, 's1', canonical_transparency_root, epoch_2, epoch_pk_2,
                             lineage_root_2, 'current', 'active', 'canonical'
   ) @ #ia)
 ∧
  (#i0 < #it1) ∧ (#it1 < #it2) ∧ (#it2 < #ia)"
*/
by sorry

lemma executable_generalized_revocation_exception_lifecycle:
  exists-trace
  "∃ verifier contract child_id certificate log canonical_transparency_root
     epoch_0 epoch_pk_0 lineage_root_0 #i0 #iepoch_compromise #irevoke
     #imissing #iaccept_missing #iapply #irevocation_compromise
     #iaccept_compromised.
    ((((((((((((((GeneralizedSecurityCompositionInitialized( verifier,
                                                             contract, child_id, certificate, log, 's1',
                                                             canonical_transparency_root, epoch_0, epoch_pk_0,
                                                             lineage_root_0
                  ) @ #i0) ∧
                 (GeneralizedCompositionVerifierCompromised( verifier, contract, epoch_0
                  ) @ #iepoch_compromise)) ∧
                (GeneralizedCertificateRevoked( verifier, certificate ) @ #irevoke)) ∧
               (GeneralizedRevocationUpdateMissing( verifier, certificate
                ) @ #imissing)) ∧
              (GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                                         log, 's1', canonical_transparency_root, epoch_0, epoch_pk_0,
                                         lineage_root_0, 'stale', 'revoked-missing-update', 'canonical'
               ) @ #iaccept_missing)) ∧
             (GeneralizedCurrentRevocationStateApplied( verifier, certificate
              ) @ #iapply)) ∧
            (GeneralizedRevocationVerifierCompromised( verifier, certificate
             ) @ #irevocation_compromise)) ∧
           (GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                                      log, 's1', canonical_transparency_root, epoch_0, epoch_pk_0,
                                      lineage_root_0, 'stale', 'revoked-compromised-verifier', 'canonical'
            ) @ #iaccept_compromised)) ∧
          (#i0 < #iepoch_compromise)) ∧
         (#iepoch_compromise < #irevoke)) ∧
        (#irevoke < #imissing)) ∧
       (#imissing < #iaccept_missing)) ∧
      (#iaccept_missing < #iapply)) ∧
     (#iapply < #irevocation_compromise)) ∧
    (#irevocation_compromise < #iaccept_compromised)"
/*
guarded formula characterizing all satisfying traces:
"∃ verifier contract child_id certificate log canonical_transparency_root
   epoch_0 epoch_pk_0 lineage_root_0 #i0 #iepoch_compromise #irevoke
   #imissing #iaccept_missing #iapply #irevocation_compromise
   #iaccept_compromised.
  (GeneralizedSecurityCompositionInitialized( verifier, contract, child_id,
                                              certificate, log, 's1', canonical_transparency_root, epoch_0,
                                              epoch_pk_0, lineage_root_0
   ) @ #i0) ∧
  (GeneralizedCompositionVerifierCompromised( verifier, contract, epoch_0
   ) @ #iepoch_compromise) ∧
  (GeneralizedCertificateRevoked( verifier, certificate ) @ #irevoke) ∧
  (GeneralizedRevocationUpdateMissing( verifier, certificate
   ) @ #imissing) ∧
  (GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                             log, 's1', canonical_transparency_root, epoch_0, epoch_pk_0,
                             lineage_root_0, 'stale', 'revoked-missing-update', 'canonical'
   ) @ #iaccept_missing) ∧
  (GeneralizedCurrentRevocationStateApplied( verifier, certificate
   ) @ #iapply) ∧
  (GeneralizedRevocationVerifierCompromised( verifier, certificate
   ) @ #irevocation_compromise) ∧
  (GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                             log, 's1', canonical_transparency_root, epoch_0, epoch_pk_0,
                             lineage_root_0, 'stale', 'revoked-compromised-verifier', 'canonical'
   ) @ #iaccept_compromised)
 ∧
  (#i0 < #iepoch_compromise) ∧
  (#iepoch_compromise < #irevoke) ∧
  (#irevoke < #imissing) ∧
  (#imissing < #iaccept_missing) ∧
  (#iaccept_missing < #iapply) ∧
  (#iapply < #irevocation_compromise) ∧
  (#irevocation_compromise < #iaccept_compromised)"
*/
by sorry

lemma generalized_acceptance_requires_c5c_and_c6a_contracts:
  all-traces
  "∀ verifier contract child_id certificate log checkpoint
     transparency_root epoch epoch_pk lineage_root epoch_mode revocation_mode
     transparency_mode #ia.
    (GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                               log, checkpoint, transparency_root, epoch, epoch_pk, lineage_root,
                               epoch_mode, revocation_mode, transparency_mode
     ) @ #ia) ⇒
    (∃ canonical_root initial_epoch initial_epoch_pk initial_lineage_root
       #ic5c #ic6a.
      (((C5CContractImported( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate, log,
                              checkpoint, canonical_root
         ) @ #ic5c) ∧
        (C6AContractImported( verifier, contract, initial_epoch,
                              initial_epoch_pk, initial_lineage_root
         ) @ #ic6a)) ∧
       (#ic5c < #ia)) ∧
      (#ic6a < #ia))"
/*
guarded formula characterizing all counter-examples:
"∃ verifier contract child_id certificate log checkpoint
   transparency_root epoch epoch_pk lineage_root epoch_mode revocation_mode
   transparency_mode #ia.
  (GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                             log, checkpoint, transparency_root, epoch, epoch_pk, lineage_root,
                             epoch_mode, revocation_mode, transparency_mode
   ) @ #ia)
 ∧
  ∀ canonical_root initial_epoch initial_epoch_pk initial_lineage_root
    #ic5c #ic6a.
   (C5CContractImported( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate, log,
                         checkpoint, canonical_root
    ) @ #ic5c) ∧
   (C6AContractImported( verifier, contract, initial_epoch,
                         initial_epoch_pk, initial_lineage_root
    ) @ #ic6a)
  ⇒
   ((¬(#ic5c < #ia)) ∨ (¬(#ic6a < #ia)))"
*/
by sorry

  "∀ verifier contract child_id certificate log checkpoint
     transparency_root epoch epoch_pk lineage_root #ia.

      ) @ #ia) ∧
     (GeneralizedSecurityComponentSatisfied( verifier, contract, child_id,
                                             certificate, log, checkpoint, transparency_root, 'active',
                                             'canonical'
      ) @ #ia))"

guarded formula characterizing all counter-examples:
"∃ verifier contract child_id certificate log checkpoint
   transparency_root epoch epoch_pk lineage_root #ia.
  (GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                             log, checkpoint, transparency_root, epoch, epoch_pk, lineage_root,
                             'current', 'active', 'canonical'
   ) @ #ia)
 ∧

                                          epoch_pk, lineage_root, 'current'

   (¬(GeneralizedSecurityComponentSatisfied( verifier, contract, child_id,
                                             certificate, log, checkpoint, transparency_root, 'active',
                                             'canonical'
      ) @ #ia)))"
*/
by sorry

lemma generalized_epoch_compromise_use_requires_prior_compromise:
  all-traces
  "∀ verifier contract epoch #iu.
    (GeneralizedEpochCompromiseUsed( verifier, contract, epoch ) @ #iu) ⇒
    (∃ compromise_epoch #ic.
      (GeneralizedCompositionVerifierCompromised( verifier, contract,
                                                  compromise_epoch
       ) @ #ic) ∧
      (#ic < #iu))"
/*
guarded formula characterizing all counter-examples:
"∃ verifier contract epoch #iu.
  (GeneralizedEpochCompromiseUsed( verifier, contract, epoch ) @ #iu)
 ∧
  ∀ compromise_epoch #ic.
   (GeneralizedCompositionVerifierCompromised( verifier, contract,
                                               compromise_epoch
    ) @ #ic)
  ⇒
   ¬(#ic < #iu)"
*/
simplify
solve( GeneralizedEpochCompromiseUsed( verifier, contract, epoch
       ) @ #iu )
  case Accept_Revoked_Generalized_Composition_After_Verifier_Compromise
  solve( !C5CSecurityContract( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                               log, checkpoint, canonical_transparency_root
         ) ▶₀ #iu )
    case Import_Verified_C5C_And_C6A_Contracts
    solve( !C6AMultiEpochContract( ~verifier, ~contract ) ▶₁ #iu )
      case Import_Verified_C5C_And_C6A_Contracts
      solve( !GeneralizedCompromisedRevocationContract( ~verifier, ~certificate
             ) ▶₂ #iu )
        case Compromise_Generalized_Revocation_Verifier_case_1
        solve( !GeneralizedCompositionCompromiseState( ~verifier, ~contract
               ) ▶₄ #iu )
          case Compromise_Generalized_Composition_Verifier_case_1
          by contradiction /* from formulas */
        next
          case Compromise_Generalized_Composition_Verifier_case_2
          by contradiction /* from formulas */
        next
          case Compromise_Generalized_Composition_Verifier_case_3
          by contradiction /* from formulas */
        next
          case Compromise_Generalized_Composition_Verifier_case_4
          by contradiction /* from formulas */
        next
          case Compromise_Generalized_Composition_Verifier_case_5
          by contradiction /* from formulas */
        qed
      next
        case Compromise_Generalized_Revocation_Verifier_case_2
        solve( !GeneralizedCompositionCompromiseState( ~verifier, ~contract
               ) ▶₄ #iu )
          case Compromise_Generalized_Composition_Verifier_case_1
          by contradiction /* from formulas */
        next
          case Compromise_Generalized_Composition_Verifier_case_2
          by contradiction /* from formulas */
        next
          case Compromise_Generalized_Composition_Verifier_case_3
          by contradiction /* from formulas */
        next
          case Compromise_Generalized_Composition_Verifier_case_4
          by contradiction /* from formulas */
        next
          case Compromise_Generalized_Composition_Verifier_case_5
          by contradiction /* from formulas */
        qed
      next
        case Compromise_Generalized_Revocation_Verifier_case_3
        solve( !GeneralizedCompositionCompromiseState( ~verifier, ~contract
               ) ▶₄ #iu )
          case Compromise_Generalized_Composition_Verifier_case_1
          by contradiction /* from formulas */
        next
          case Compromise_Generalized_Composition_Verifier_case_2
          by contradiction /* from formulas */
        next
          case Compromise_Generalized_Composition_Verifier_case_3
          by contradiction /* from formulas */
        next
          case Compromise_Generalized_Composition_Verifier_case_4
          by contradiction /* from formulas */
        next
          case Compromise_Generalized_Composition_Verifier_case_5
          by contradiction /* from formulas */
        qed
      next
        case Compromise_Generalized_Revocation_Verifier_case_4
        solve( !GeneralizedCompositionCompromiseState( ~verifier, ~contract
               ) ▶₄ #iu )
          case Compromise_Generalized_Composition_Verifier_case_1
          by contradiction /* from formulas */
        next
          case Compromise_Generalized_Composition_Verifier_case_2
          by contradiction /* from formulas */
        next
          case Compromise_Generalized_Composition_Verifier_case_3
          by contradiction /* from formulas */
        next
          case Compromise_Generalized_Composition_Verifier_case_4
          by contradiction /* from formulas */
        next
          case Compromise_Generalized_Composition_Verifier_case_5
          by contradiction /* from formulas */
        qed
      next
        case Compromise_Generalized_Revocation_Verifier_case_5
        by contradiction /* from formulas */
      next
        case Compromise_Generalized_Revocation_Verifier_case_6
        by contradiction /* from formulas */
      next
        case Compromise_Generalized_Revocation_Verifier_case_7
        by contradiction /* from formulas */
      next
        case Compromise_Generalized_Revocation_Verifier_case_8
        by contradiction /* from formulas */
      next
        case Compromise_Generalized_Revocation_Verifier_case_9
        by contradiction /* from formulas */
      qed
    qed
  qed
next
  case Accept_Revoked_Generalized_Composition_While_Update_Missing
  solve( !C5CSecurityContract( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                               log, checkpoint, canonical_transparency_root
         ) ▶₀ #iu )
    case Import_Verified_C5C_And_C6A_Contracts
    solve( !C6AMultiEpochContract( ~verifier, ~contract ) ▶₁ #iu )
      case Import_Verified_C5C_And_C6A_Contracts
      solve( !GeneralizedMissingUpdateContract( ~verifier, ~certificate
             ) ▶₂ #iu )
        case Observe_Generalized_Missing_Revocation_Update_case_1
        solve( !GeneralizedCompositionCompromiseState( ~verifier, ~contract
               ) ▶₄ #iu )
          case Compromise_Generalized_Composition_Verifier_case_1
          by contradiction /* from formulas */
        next
          case Compromise_Generalized_Composition_Verifier_case_2
          by contradiction /* from formulas */
        next
          case Compromise_Generalized_Composition_Verifier_case_3
          by contradiction /* from formulas */
        next
          case Compromise_Generalized_Composition_Verifier_case_4
          by contradiction /* from formulas */
        next
          case Compromise_Generalized_Composition_Verifier_case_5
          by contradiction /* from formulas */
        qed
      next
        case Observe_Generalized_Missing_Revocation_Update_case_2
        solve( !GeneralizedCompositionCompromiseState( ~verifier, ~contract
               ) ▶₄ #iu )
          case Compromise_Generalized_Composition_Verifier_case_1

lemma revoked_generalized_acceptance_requires_explicit_exception:
  all-traces
  "∀ verifier contract child_id certificate log checkpoint
     transparency_root epoch epoch_pk lineage_root epoch_mode revocation_mode
     transparency_mode #ia.
    ((GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                                log, checkpoint, transparency_root, epoch, epoch_pk, lineage_root,
                                epoch_mode, revocation_mode, transparency_mode
      ) @ #ia) ∧
     (¬(revocation_mode = 'active'))) ⇒
    ((∃ #im.
       (GeneralizedRevocationUpdateMissing( verifier, certificate ) @ #im) ∧
       (#im < #ia)) ∨
     (∃ #ic.
       (GeneralizedRevocationVerifierCompromised( verifier, certificate
        ) @ #ic) ∧
       (#ic < #ia)))"

  /* has exactly the trivial AC variant */

rule (modulo E) Accept_Revoked_Generalized_Composition_While_Update_Missing:
   [
   !C5CSecurityContract( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate, log,
                         checkpoint, canonical_transparency_root
   ),
   !C6AMultiEpochContract( verifier, contract ),
   !GeneralizedMissingUpdateContract( verifier, certificate ),
   GeneralizedCompositionEpochState( verifier, contract, epoch, epoch_pk,
                                     lineage_root, 'compromised'
   ),
   !GeneralizedCompositionCompromiseState( verifier, contract ),
   GeneralizedCertificateStatus( certificate, 'revoked' ),
   MissingUpdateGeneralizedAcceptancePermit( verifier, certificate )
   ]
  --[
  GeneralizedEpochCompromiseUsed( verifier, contract, epoch ),
  GeneralizedEpochComponentSatisfied( verifier, contract, epoch, epoch_pk,
                                      lineage_root, 'stale'
  ),
  GeneralizedSecurityComponentSatisfied( verifier, contract, child_id,
                                         certificate, log, checkpoint, canonical_transparency_root,
                                         'revoked-missing-update', 'canonical'
  ),
  GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate, log,
                            checkpoint, canonical_transparency_root, epoch, epoch_pk, lineage_root,
                            'stale', 'revoked-missing-update', 'canonical'
  )
  ]->
   [
   GeneralizedCompositionEpochState( verifier, contract, epoch, epoch_pk,
                                     lineage_root, 'compromised'
   ),
   GeneralizedCertificateStatus( certificate, 'revoked' )
   ]

  // loop breakers: [3,5]
  /* has exactly the trivial AC variant */

rule (modulo E) Apply_Generalized_Revocation_Update:
   [
   GeneralizedCertificateStatus( certificate, 'revoked' ),
   ApplyGeneralizedRevocationUpdatePermit( verifier, certificate )
   ]
  --[ GeneralizedCurrentRevocationStateApplied( verifier, certificate ) ]->
   [
   GeneralizedCertificateStatus( certificate, 'revoked' ),
   CompromiseGeneralizedRevocationVerifierPermit( verifier, certificate )
   ]

  // loop breaker: [0]
  /* has exactly the trivial AC variant */

rule (modulo E) Compromise_Generalized_Revocation_Verifier:
   [ CompromiseGeneralizedRevocationVerifierPermit( verifier, certificate )
   ]
  --[ GeneralizedRevocationVerifierCompromised( verifier, certificate ) ]->
   [
   !GeneralizedCompromisedRevocationContract( verifier, certificate ),
   CompromisedRevocationGeneralizedAcceptancePermit( verifier, certificate )
   ]

  /* has exactly the trivial AC variant */

rule (modulo E) Accept_Revoked_Generalized_Composition_After_Verifier_Compromise:
   [
   !C5CSecurityContract( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate, log,
                         checkpoint, canonical_transparency_root
   ),
   !C6AMultiEpochContract( verifier, contract ),
   !GeneralizedCompromisedRevocationContract( verifier, certificate ),
   GeneralizedCompositionEpochState( verifier, contract, epoch, epoch_pk,
                                     lineage_root, 'compromised'
   ),
   !GeneralizedCompositionCompromiseState( verifier, contract ),
   GeneralizedCertificateStatus( certificate, 'revoked' ),
   CompromisedRevocationGeneralizedAcceptancePermit( verifier, certificate )
   ]
  --[
  GeneralizedEpochCompromiseUsed( verifier, contract, epoch ),
  GeneralizedEpochComponentSatisfied( verifier, contract, epoch, epoch_pk,
                                      lineage_root, 'stale'
  ),
  GeneralizedSecurityComponentSatisfied( verifier, contract, child_id,
                                         certificate, log, checkpoint, canonical_transparency_root,
                                         'revoked-compromised-verifier', 'canonical'
  ),
  GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate, log,
                            checkpoint, canonical_transparency_root, epoch, epoch_pk, lineage_root,
                            'stale', 'revoked-compromised-verifier', 'canonical'
  )
  ]->
   [
   GeneralizedCompositionEpochState( verifier, contract, epoch, epoch_pk,
                                     lineage_root, 'compromised'
   ),
   GeneralizedCertificateStatus( certificate, 'revoked' )
   ]

  // loop breakers: [3,5]
  /* has exactly the trivial AC variant */

lemma executable_generalized_clean_multi_epoch_lifecycle:
  exists-trace
  "∃ verifier contract child_id certificate log canonical_transparency_root
     epoch_0 epoch_pk_0 lineage_root_0 epoch_1 epoch_2 epoch_pk_2
     lineage_root_2 #i0 #it1 #it2 #ia.
    ((((((GeneralizedSecurityCompositionInitialized( verifier, contract,
                                                     child_id, certificate, log, 's1',
                                                     canonical_transparency_root, epoch_0, epoch_pk_0,
                                                     lineage_root_0
          ) @ #i0) ∧
         (GeneralizedCompositionEpochTransition( contract, epoch_0, epoch_1
          ) @ #it1)) ∧
        (GeneralizedCompositionEpochTransition( contract, epoch_1, epoch_2
         ) @ #it2)) ∧
       (GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                                  log, 's1', canonical_transparency_root, epoch_2, epoch_pk_2,
                                  lineage_root_2, 'current', 'active', 'canonical'
        ) @ #ia)) ∧
      (#i0 < #it1)) ∧
     (#it1 < #it2)) ∧
    (#it2 < #ia)"
/*
guarded formula characterizing all satisfying traces:
"∃ verifier contract child_id certificate log canonical_transparency_root
   epoch_0 epoch_pk_0 lineage_root_0 epoch_1 epoch_2 epoch_pk_2
   lineage_root_2 #i0 #it1 #it2 #ia.
  (GeneralizedSecurityCompositionInitialized( verifier, contract, child_id,
                                              certificate, log, 's1', canonical_transparency_root, epoch_0,
                                              epoch_pk_0, lineage_root_0
   ) @ #i0) ∧
  (GeneralizedCompositionEpochTransition( contract, epoch_0, epoch_1
   ) @ #it1) ∧
  (GeneralizedCompositionEpochTransition( contract, epoch_1, epoch_2
   ) @ #it2) ∧
  (GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                             log, 's1', canonical_transparency_root, epoch_2, epoch_pk_2,
                             lineage_root_2, 'current', 'active', 'canonical'
   ) @ #ia)
 ∧
  (#i0 < #it1) ∧ (#it1 < #it2) ∧ (#it2 < #ia)"
*/
by sorry

lemma executable_generalized_revocation_exception_lifecycle:
  exists-trace
  "∃ verifier contract child_id certificate log canonical_transparency_root
     epoch_0 epoch_pk_0 lineage_root_0 #i0 #iepoch_compromise #irevoke
     #imissing #iaccept_missing #iapply #irevocation_compromise
     #iaccept_compromised.
    ((((((((((((((GeneralizedSecurityCompositionInitialized( verifier,
                                                             contract, child_id, certificate, log, 's1',
                                                             canonical_transparency_root, epoch_0, epoch_pk_0,
                                                             lineage_root_0
                  ) @ #i0) ∧
                 (GeneralizedCompositionVerifierCompromised( verifier, contract, epoch_0
                  ) @ #iepoch_compromise)) ∧
                (GeneralizedCertificateRevoked( verifier, certificate ) @ #irevoke)) ∧
               (GeneralizedRevocationUpdateMissing( verifier, certificate
                ) @ #imissing)) ∧
              (GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                                         log, 's1', canonical_transparency_root, epoch_0, epoch_pk_0,
                                         lineage_root_0, 'stale', 'revoked-missing-update', 'canonical'
               ) @ #iaccept_missing)) ∧
             (GeneralizedCurrentRevocationStateApplied( verifier, certificate
              ) @ #iapply)) ∧
            (GeneralizedRevocationVerifierCompromised( verifier, certificate
             ) @ #irevocation_compromise)) ∧
           (GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                                      log, 's1', canonical_transparency_root, epoch_0, epoch_pk_0,
                                      lineage_root_0, 'stale', 'revoked-compromised-verifier', 'canonical'
            ) @ #iaccept_compromised)) ∧
          (#i0 < #iepoch_compromise)) ∧
         (#iepoch_compromise < #irevoke)) ∧
        (#irevoke < #imissing)) ∧
       (#imissing < #iaccept_missing)) ∧
      (#iaccept_missing < #iapply)) ∧
     (#iapply < #irevocation_compromise)) ∧
    (#irevocation_compromise < #iaccept_compromised)"
/*
guarded formula characterizing all satisfying traces:
"∃ verifier contract child_id certificate log canonical_transparency_root
   epoch_0 epoch_pk_0 lineage_root_0 #i0 #iepoch_compromise #irevoke
   #imissing #iaccept_missing #iapply #irevocation_compromise
   #iaccept_compromised.
  (GeneralizedSecurityCompositionInitialized( verifier, contract, child_id,
                                              certificate, log, 's1', canonical_transparency_root, epoch_0,
                                              epoch_pk_0, lineage_root_0
   ) @ #i0) ∧
  (GeneralizedCompositionVerifierCompromised( verifier, contract, epoch_0
   ) @ #iepoch_compromise) ∧
  (GeneralizedCertificateRevoked( verifier, certificate ) @ #irevoke) ∧
  (GeneralizedRevocationUpdateMissing( verifier, certificate
   ) @ #imissing) ∧
  (GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                             log, 's1', canonical_transparency_root, epoch_0, epoch_pk_0,
                             lineage_root_0, 'stale', 'revoked-missing-update', 'canonical'
   ) @ #iaccept_missing) ∧
  (GeneralizedCurrentRevocationStateApplied( verifier, certificate
   ) @ #iapply) ∧
  (GeneralizedRevocationVerifierCompromised( verifier, certificate
   ) @ #irevocation_compromise) ∧
  (GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                             log, 's1', canonical_transparency_root, epoch_0, epoch_pk_0,
                             lineage_root_0, 'stale', 'revoked-compromised-verifier', 'canonical'
   ) @ #iaccept_compromised)
 ∧
  (#i0 < #iepoch_compromise) ∧
  (#iepoch_compromise < #irevoke) ∧
  (#irevoke < #imissing) ∧
  (#imissing < #iaccept_missing) ∧
  (#iaccept_missing < #iapply) ∧
  (#iapply < #irevocation_compromise) ∧
  (#irevocation_compromise < #iaccept_compromised)"
*/
by sorry

lemma generalized_acceptance_requires_c5c_and_c6a_contracts:
  all-traces
  "∀ verifier contract child_id certificate log checkpoint
     transparency_root epoch epoch_pk lineage_root epoch_mode revocation_mode
     transparency_mode #ia.
    (GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                               log, checkpoint, transparency_root, epoch, epoch_pk, lineage_root,
                               epoch_mode, revocation_mode, transparency_mode
     ) @ #ia) ⇒
    (∃ canonical_root initial_epoch initial_epoch_pk initial_lineage_root
       #ic5c #ic6a.
      (((C5CContractImported( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate, log,
                              checkpoint, canonical_root
         ) @ #ic5c) ∧
        (C6AContractImported( verifier, contract, initial_epoch,
                              initial_epoch_pk, initial_lineage_root
         ) @ #ic6a)) ∧
       (#ic5c < #ia)) ∧
      (#ic6a < #ia))"
/*
guarded formula characterizing all counter-examples:
"∃ verifier contract child_id certificate log checkpoint
   transparency_root epoch epoch_pk lineage_root epoch_mode revocation_mode
   transparency_mode #ia.
  (GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                             log, checkpoint, transparency_root, epoch, epoch_pk, lineage_root,
                             epoch_mode, revocation_mode, transparency_mode
   ) @ #ia)
 ∧
  ∀ canonical_root initial_epoch initial_epoch_pk initial_lineage_root
    #ic5c #ic6a.
   (C5CContractImported( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate, log,
                         checkpoint, canonical_root
    ) @ #ic5c) ∧
   (C6AContractImported( verifier, contract, initial_epoch,
                         initial_epoch_pk, initial_lineage_root
    ) @ #ic6a)
  ⇒
   ((¬(#ic5c < #ia)) ∨ (¬(#ic6a < #ia)))"
*/
by sorry

lemma clean_generalized_acceptance_has_complete_evidence:
  all-traces
  "∀ verifier contract child_id certificate log checkpoint
     transparency_root epoch epoch_pk lineage_root #ia.
    (GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                               log, checkpoint, transparency_root, epoch, epoch_pk, lineage_root,
                               'current', 'active', 'canonical'
     ) @ #ia) ⇒
    ((GeneralizedEpochComponentSatisfied( verifier, contract, epoch,
                                          epoch_pk, lineage_root, 'current'
      ) @ #ia) ∧
     (GeneralizedSecurityComponentSatisfied( verifier, contract, child_id,
                                             certificate, log, checkpoint, transparency_root, 'active',
                                             'canonical'
      ) @ #ia))"
/*
guarded formula characterizing all counter-examples:
"∃ verifier contract child_id certificate log checkpoint
   transparency_root epoch epoch_pk lineage_root #ia.
  (GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                             log, checkpoint, transparency_root, epoch, epoch_pk, lineage_root,
                             'current', 'active', 'canonical'
   ) @ #ia)
 ∧
  ((¬(GeneralizedEpochComponentSatisfied( verifier, contract, epoch,
                                          epoch_pk, lineage_root, 'current'
      ) @ #ia)) ∨
   (¬(GeneralizedSecurityComponentSatisfied( verifier, contract, child_id,
                                             certificate, log, checkpoint, transparency_root, 'active',
                                             'canonical'
      ) @ #ia)))"
*/
by sorry

lemma generalized_epoch_compromise_use_requires_prior_compromise:
  all-traces
  "∀ verifier contract epoch #iu.
    (GeneralizedEpochCompromiseUsed( verifier, contract, epoch ) @ #iu) ⇒
    (∃ compromise_epoch #ic.
      (GeneralizedCompositionVerifierCompromised( verifier, contract,
                                                  compromise_epoch
       ) @ #ic) ∧
      (#ic < #iu))"
/*
guarded formula characterizing all counter-examples:
"∃ verifier contract epoch #iu.
  (GeneralizedEpochCompromiseUsed( verifier, contract, epoch ) @ #iu)
 ∧
  ∀ compromise_epoch #ic.
   (GeneralizedCompositionVerifierCompromised( verifier, contract,
                                               compromise_epoch
    ) @ #ic)
  ⇒
   ¬(#ic < #iu)"
*/
by sorry

lemma revoked_generalized_acceptance_requires_explicit_exception:
  all-traces
  "∀ verifier contract child_id certificate log checkpoint
     transparency_root epoch epoch_pk lineage_root epoch_mode revocation_mode
     transparency_mode #ia.
    ((GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                                log, checkpoint, transparency_root, epoch, epoch_pk, lineage_root,
                                epoch_mode, revocation_mode, transparency_mode
      ) @ #ia) ∧
     (¬(revocation_mode = 'active'))) ⇒
    ((∃ #im.
       (GeneralizedRevocationUpdateMissing( verifier, certificate ) @ #im) ∧
       (#im < #ia)) ∨
     (∃ #ic.
       (GeneralizedRevocationVerifierCompromised( verifier, certificate
        ) @ #ic) ∧
       (#ic < #ia)))"
/*
guarded formula characterizing all counter-examples:
"∃ verifier contract child_id certificate log checkpoint
   transparency_root epoch epoch_pk lineage_root epoch_mode revocation_mode
   transparency_mode #ia.
  (GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                             log, checkpoint, transparency_root, epoch, epoch_pk, lineage_root,
                             epoch_mode, revocation_mode, transparency_mode
   ) @ #ia)
 ∧
  (¬(revocation_mode = 'active')) ∧
  (∀ #im.
    (GeneralizedRevocationUpdateMissing( verifier, certificate ) @ #im)
   ⇒
    ¬(#im < #ia)) ∧
  (∀ #ic.
    (GeneralizedRevocationVerifierCompromised( verifier, certificate ) @ #ic)
   ⇒
    ¬(#ic < #ia))"
*/
simplify
solve( GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id,
                                 certificate, log, checkpoint, transparency_root, epoch, epoch_pk,
                                 lineage_root, epoch_mode, revocation_mode, transparency_mode
       ) @ #ia )
  case Accept_Clean_Generalized_Composition
  by contradiction /* from formulas */
next
  case Accept_Generalized_Composition_Under_Forked_Transparency
  by contradiction /* from formulas */
next
  case Accept_Revoked_Generalized_Composition_After_Verifier_Compromise
  solve( !C5CSecurityContract( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                               log, checkpoint, transparency_root
         ) ▶₀ #ia )
    case Import_Verified_C5C_And_C6A_Contracts
    solve( !C6AMultiEpochContract( ~verifier, ~contract ) ▶₁ #ia )
      case Import_Verified_C5C_And_C6A_Contracts
      solve( !GeneralizedCompromisedRevocationContract( ~verifier, ~certificate
             ) ▶₂ #ia )
        case Compromise_Generalized_Revocation_Verifier_case_1
        by contradiction /* from formulas */
      next
        case Compromise_Generalized_Revocation_Verifier_case_2
        by contradiction /* from formulas */
      next
        case Compromise_Generalized_Revocation_Verifier_case_3
        by contradiction /* from formulas */
      next
        case Compromise_Generalized_Revocation_Verifier_case_4
        by contradiction /* from formulas */
      next
        case Compromise_Generalized_Revocation_Verifier_case_5
        by contradiction /* from formulas */
      next
        case Compromise_Generalized_Revocation_Verifier_case_6
        by contradiction /* from formulas */
      next
        case Compromise_Generalized_Revocation_Verifier_case_7
        by contradiction /* from formulas */
      next
        case Compromise_Generalized_Revocation_Verifier_case_8
        by contradiction /* from formulas */
      next
        case Compromise_Generalized_Revocation_Verifier_case_9
        by contradiction /* from formulas */
      qed
    qed
  qed
next
  case Accept_Revoked_Generalized_Composition_While_Update_Missing
  solve( !C5CSecurityContract( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                               log, checkpoint, transparency_root
         ) ▶₀ #ia )
    case Import_Verified_C5C_And_C6A_Contracts
    solve( !C6AMultiEpochContract( ~verifier, ~contract ) ▶₁ #ia )
      case Import_Verified_C5C_And_C6A_Contracts
      solve( !GeneralizedMissingUpdateContract( ~verifier, ~certificate
             ) ▶₂ #ia )
        case Observe_Generalized_Missing_Revocation_Update_case_1
        by contradiction /* from formulas */
      next
        case Observe_Generalized_Missing_Revocation_Update_case_2
        by contradiction /* from formulas */
      next
        case Observe_Generalized_Missing_Revocation_Update_case_3
        by contradiction /* from formulas */
      next
        case Observe_Generalized_Missing_Revocation_Update_case_4
        by contradiction /* from formulas */
      next
        case Observe_Generalized_Missing_Revocation_Update_case_5
        by contradiction /* from formulas */
      next
        case Observe_Generalized_Missing_Revocation_Update_case_6
        by contradiction /* from formulas */
      next
        case Observe_Generalized_Missing_Revocation_Update_case_7
        by contradiction /* from formulas */
      next
        case Observe_Generalized_Missing_Revocation_Update_case_8
        by contradiction /* from formulas */
      next
        case Observe_Generalized_Missing_Revocation_Update_case_9
        by contradiction /* from formulas */
      qed
    qed
  qed
next
  case Accept_Stale_Generalized_Composition
  by contradiction /* from formulas */
qed

lemma forked_generalized_acceptance_requires_prior_log_compromise:
  all-traces
  "∀ verifier contract child_id certificate log checkpoint

lemma executable_generalized_clean_multi_epoch_lifecycle:
  exists-trace
  "∃ verifier contract child_id certificate log canonical_transparency_root
     epoch_0 epoch_pk_0 lineage_root_0 epoch_1 epoch_2 epoch_pk_2
     lineage_root_2 #i0 #it1 #it2 #ia.
    ((((((GeneralizedSecurityCompositionInitialized( verifier, contract,
                                                     child_id, certificate, log, 's1',
                                                     canonical_transparency_root, epoch_0, epoch_pk_0,
                                                     lineage_root_0
          ) @ #i0) ∧
         (GeneralizedCompositionEpochTransition( contract, epoch_0, epoch_1
          ) @ #it1)) ∧
        (GeneralizedCompositionEpochTransition( contract, epoch_1, epoch_2
         ) @ #it2)) ∧
       (GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                                  log, 's1', canonical_transparency_root, epoch_2, epoch_pk_2,
                                  lineage_root_2, 'current', 'active', 'canonical'
        ) @ #ia)) ∧
      (#i0 < #it1)) ∧
     (#it1 < #it2)) ∧
    (#it2 < #ia)"
/*

lemma executable_generalized_revocation_exception_lifecycle:
  exists-trace
  "∃ verifier contract child_id certificate log canonical_transparency_root
     epoch_0 epoch_pk_0 lineage_root_0 #i0 #iepoch_compromise #irevoke
     #imissing #iaccept_missing #iapply #irevocation_compromise
     #iaccept_compromised.
    ((((((((((((((GeneralizedSecurityCompositionInitialized( verifier,
                                                             contract, child_id, certificate, log, 's1',
                                                             canonical_transparency_root, epoch_0, epoch_pk_0,
                                                             lineage_root_0
                  ) @ #i0) ∧
                 (GeneralizedCompositionVerifierCompromised( verifier, contract, epoch_0
                  ) @ #iepoch_compromise)) ∧
                (GeneralizedCertificateRevoked( verifier, certificate ) @ #irevoke)) ∧
               (GeneralizedRevocationUpdateMissing( verifier, certificate
                ) @ #imissing)) ∧
              (GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                                         log, 's1', canonical_transparency_root, epoch_0, epoch_pk_0,
                                         lineage_root_0, 'stale', 'revoked-missing-update', 'canonical'
               ) @ #iaccept_missing)) ∧
             (GeneralizedCurrentRevocationStateApplied( verifier, certificate
              ) @ #iapply)) ∧
            (GeneralizedRevocationVerifierCompromised( verifier, certificate
             ) @ #irevocation_compromise)) ∧
           (GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                                      log, 's1', canonical_transparency_root, epoch_0, epoch_pk_0,
                                      lineage_root_0, 'stale', 'revoked-compromised-verifier', 'canonical'
            ) @ #iaccept_compromised)) ∧
          (#i0 < #iepoch_compromise)) ∧
         (#iepoch_compromise < #irevoke)) ∧
        (#irevoke < #imissing)) ∧
       (#imissing < #iaccept_missing)) ∧
      (#iaccept_missing < #iapply)) ∧
     (#iapply < #irevocation_compromise)) ∧
    (#irevocation_compromise < #iaccept_compromised)"

  all-traces
  "∀ verifier contract child_id certificate log checkpoint
     transparency_root epoch epoch_pk lineage_root epoch_mode revocation_mode
     transparency_mode #ia.

                               log, checkpoint, transparency_root, epoch, epoch_pk, lineage_root,
                               epoch_mode, revocation_mode, transparency_mode

       #ic5c #ic6a.

                              checkpoint, canonical_root

                              initial_epoch_pk, initial_lineage_root
         ) @ #ic6a)) ∧

lemma forked_generalized_acceptance_requires_prior_log_compromise:
  all-traces
  "∀ verifier contract child_id certificate log checkpoint
     transparency_root epoch epoch_pk lineage_root epoch_mode revocation_mode
     #ia.
    (GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                               log, checkpoint, transparency_root, epoch, epoch_pk, lineage_root,
                               epoch_mode, revocation_mode, 'forked'
     ) @ #ia) ⇒
    (∃ canonical_root #ic.
      (GeneralizedTransparencyLogCompromised( log, checkpoint, canonical_root
       ) @ #ic) ∧
      (#ic < #ia))"
/*
guarded formula characterizing all counter-examples:
"∃ verifier contract child_id certificate log checkpoint
   transparency_root epoch epoch_pk lineage_root epoch_mode revocation_mode
   #ia.
  (GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                             log, checkpoint, transparency_root, epoch, epoch_pk, lineage_root,
                             epoch_mode, revocation_mode, 'forked'
   ) @ #ia)
 ∧
  ∀ canonical_root #ic.
   (GeneralizedTransparencyLogCompromised( log, checkpoint, canonical_root
    ) @ #ic)
  ⇒
   ¬(#ic < #ia)"
*/
simplify
solve( GeneralizedFinalAccepted( verifier, contract, child_id,
                                 certificate, log, checkpoint, transparency_root, epoch, epoch_pk,
                                 lineage_root, epoch_mode, revocation_mode, 'forked'
       ) @ #ia )
  case Accept_Generalized_Composition_Under_Forked_Transparency
  solve( !C5CSecurityContract( verifier, contract, child_id, certificate,
                               log, checkpoint, canonical_transparency_root
         ) ▶₀ #ia )
    case Import_Verified_C5C_And_C6A_Contracts
    solve( !C6AMultiEpochContract( ~verifier, ~contract ) ▶₁ #ia )
      case Import_Verified_C5C_And_C6A_Contracts
      solve( !GeneralizedForkedTransparencyContract( ~certificate, ~log, 's1',
                                                     ~canonical_transparency_root, transparency_root
             ) ▶₂ #ia )
        case Compromise_Generalized_Transparency_Log
        by contradiction /* from formulas */
      qed
    qed
  qed
qed
